1: import calendar 
2: from openpyxl import Workbook 
3: from openpyxl.styles import Alignment, Font, PatternFill, Border, Side 
4: from openpyxl.utils import get_column_letter 
5: def export_schedule_to_excel(schedule, year, month, path): 
6:     wb = Workbook() 
7:     ws = wb.active 
8:     ws.title = "Grafik" 
9:     days_in_month = calendar.monthrange(year, month)[1] 
10:     weekdays = ["Pn", "Wt", "Śr", "Cz", "Pt", "So", "Nd"] 
11:     # Style 
12:     fill_weekend = PatternFill(start_color="F2F2F2", end_color="F2F2F2", fill_type="solid") 
13:     align_center = Alignment(horizontal="center", vertical="center") 
14:     border_thin = Border(left=Side(style='thin'), right=Side(style='thin'), 
15:                          top=Side(style='thin'), bottom=Side(style='thin')) 
16:     # NAGŁÓWEK 
17:     ws.merge_cells("A1:B2") 
18:     ws.cell(row=1, column=1, value="Nazwisko i imię").alignment = align_center 
19:      
20:     # Nagłówki dni 
21:     for day in range(1, days_in_month + 1): 
22:         col = day + 2 
23:         wd = calendar.weekday(year, month, day) 
24:         ws.cell(row=1, column=col, value=day).alignment = align_center 
25:         ws.cell(row=2, column=col, value=weekdays[wd]).alignment = align_center 
26:         if wd >= 5: 
27:             ws.cell(row=1, column=col).fill = fill_weekend 
28:             ws.cell(row=2, column=col).fill = fill_weekend 
29:     # NAGŁÓWKI PODSUMOWANIA (ostatnie kolumny) 
30:     sum_col_start = days_in_month + 3 
31:     sum_labels = ["Godziny pracy", "Urlop", "Inne", "RAZEM"] 
32:     for i, lbl in enumerate(sum_labels): 
33:         col = sum_col_start + i 
34:         ws.merge_cells(start_row=1, start_column=col, end_row=2, end_column=col) 
35:         c = ws.cell(row=1, column=col, value=lbl) 
36:         c.alignment = Alignment(textRotation=90, horizontal="center", vertical="center") 
37:         c.font = Font(bold=True) 
38:     # DANE PRACOWNIKÓW 
39:     cur_row = 3 
40:     for emp in schedule.employees: 
41:         # Scalone nazwisko 
42:         ws.merge_cells(start_row=cur_row, start_column=1, end_row=cur_row+2, end_column=1) 
43:         name_cell = ws.cell(row=cur_row, column=1, value=emp.display_name()) 
44:         name_cell.alignment = Alignment(horizontal="left", vertical="center", indent=1) 
45:         name_cell.font = Font(bold=True) 
46:         for i, lbl in enumerate(["od", "do", "h"]): 
47:             ws.cell(row=cur_row + i, column=2, value=lbl).alignment = align_center 
48:         # Dni miesiąca 
49:         for day in range(1, days_in_month + 1): 
50:             col = day + 2 
51:             ds = schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
52:             wd = calendar.weekday(year, month, day) 
53:              
54:             cells = [ws.cell(row=cur_row + i, column=col) for i in range(3)] 
55:             for c in cells: 
56:                 c.alignment = align_center 
57:                 if wd >= 5: c.fill = fill_weekend 
58:             if ds.is_leave: 
59:                 ws.merge_cells(start_row=cur_row, start_column=col, end_row=cur_row+2, end_column=col) 
60:                 cells[0].value = "URL" 
61:             elif not ds.is_empty(): 
62:                 cells[0].value = ds.start 
63:                 cells[1].value = ds.end 
64:                 cells[2].value = ds.total_as_str() 
65:         # PODSUMOWANIE W WIERSZU (na prawo) 
66:         # Godziny pracy (suma h) 
67:         ws.merge_cells(start_row=cur_row, start_column=sum_col_start, end_row=cur_row+2, end_column=sum_col_start) 
68:         ws.cell(row=cur_row, column=sum_col_start, value=schedule.total_hours_for_employee(emp)).alignment = align_center 
69:          
70:         # Urlop 
71:         ws.merge_cells(start_row=cur_row, start_column=sum_col_start+1, end_row=cur_row+2, end_column=sum_col_start+1) 
72:         ws.cell(row=cur_row, column=sum_col_start+1, value=schedule.leave_hours_for_employee(emp)).alignment = align_center 
73:          
74:         # Inne (na razie 0) 
75:         ws.merge_cells(start_row=cur_row, start_column=sum_col_start+2, end_row=cur_row+2, end_column=sum_col_start+2) 
76:         ws.cell(row=cur_row, column=sum_col_start+2, value="0").alignment = align_center 
77:          
78:         # RAZEM 
79:         ws.merge_cells(start_row=cur_row, start_column=sum_col_start+3, end_row=cur_row+2, end_column=sum_col_start+3) 
80:         ws.cell(row=cur_row, column=sum_col_start+3, value=schedule.total_with_leave_for_employee(emp)).alignment = align_center 
81:         cur_row += 3 
82:     # Krawędzie i szerokości 
83:     ws.column_dimensions["A"].width = 25 
84:     ws.column_dimensions["B"].width = 5 
85:     for col_idx in range(1, sum_col_start + 4): 
86:         col_ltr = get_column_letter(col_idx) 
87:         if col_idx > 2: ws.column_dimensions[col_ltr].width = 6 
88:         for r_idx in range(1, cur_row): 
89:             ws.cell(row=r_idx, column=col_idx).border = border_thin 
90:     wb.save(path)

1: import calendar 
2: from PIL import Image, ImageDraw, ImageFont 
3: def export_schedule_to_image(schedule, year, month, path): 
4:     days = calendar.monthrange(year, month)[1] 
5:     employees = schedule.employees 
6:     NAME_COL_W = 200 
7:     LBL_COL_W = 40 
8:     CELL_W = 60 
9:     CELL_H = 25 
10:     HEADER_H = 120 
11:     FOOTER_H = 180 
12:     width = NAME_COL_W + LBL_COL_W + (days * CELL_W) + 20 
13:     height = HEADER_H + (len(employees) * CELL_H * 3) + FOOTER_H 
14:     img = Image.new("RGB", (width, height), (255, 255, 255)) 
15:     draw = ImageDraw.Draw(img) 
16:     try: 
17:         font_r = ImageFont.truetype("arial.ttf", 14) 
18:         font_b = ImageFont.truetype("arial.ttf", 16) 
19:         font_sm = ImageFont.truetype("arial.ttf", 12) 
20:     except: 
21:         font_r = ImageFont.load_default() 
22:         font_b = font_r 
23:         font_sm = font_r 
24:     C_GRID = (160, 160, 160) 
25:     C_TEXT = (0, 0, 0) 
26:     C_HEADER_BG = (245, 245, 245) 
27:     C_WEEKEND_BG = (230, 230, 230) 
28:     # HEADER 
29:     draw.text((200, 30), f"Grafik planowany: {month:02d}/{year}", fill=C_TEXT, font=font_b) 
30:     draw.rectangle([0, HEADER_H - 60, width, HEADER_H], fill=C_HEADER_BG, outline=C_GRID, width=1) 
31:     draw.text((10, HEADER_H - 45), "Nazwisko i imię", fill=C_TEXT, font=font_b) 
32:     for d in range(1, days + 1): 
33:         x = NAME_COL_W + LBL_COL_W + (d - 1) * CELL_W 
34:         wd = calendar.weekday(year, month, d) 
35:         # weekend tylko w headerze (a nie cała kolumna) 
36:         if wd >= 5: 
37:             draw.rectangle([x, HEADER_H - 60, x + CELL_W, HEADER_H], fill=C_WEEKEND_BG) 
38:         draw.rectangle([x, HEADER_H - 60, x + CELL_W, HEADER_H - 30], outline=C_GRID) 
39:         draw.text((x + 20, HEADER_H - 55), str(d), fill=C_TEXT, font=font_b) 
40:         draw.rectangle([x, HEADER_H - 30, x + CELL_W, HEADER_H], outline=C_GRID) 
41:         draw.text((x + 12, HEADER_H - 25), ["Pn", "Wt", "Śr", "Cz", "Pt", "So", "Nd"][wd], fill=C_TEXT, font=font_r) 
42:     total_m_hours = 0 
43:     total_m_leave = 0 
44:     y_off = HEADER_H 
45:     for emp in employees: 
46:         draw.rectangle([0, y_off, NAME_COL_W, y_off + 3 * CELL_H], outline=C_GRID) 
47:         draw.text((10, y_off + CELL_H), emp.display_name(), fill=C_TEXT, font=font_b) 
48:         for i, lbl in enumerate(["od", "do", "h"]): 
49:             draw.rectangle( 
50:                 [NAME_COL_W, y_off + i * CELL_H, NAME_COL_W + LBL_COL_W, y_off + (i + 1) * CELL_H], 
51:                 outline=C_GRID 
52:             ) 
53:             draw.text((NAME_COL_W + 10, y_off + i * CELL_H + 5), lbl, fill=C_TEXT, font=font_r) 
54:         for d in range(1, days + 1): 
55:             x = NAME_COL_W + LBL_COL_W + (d - 1) * CELL_W 
56:             ds = schedule.get_day(emp, d) 
57:             for i in range(3): 
58:                 draw.rectangle([x, y_off + i * CELL_H, x + CELL_W, y_off + (i + 1) * CELL_H], outline=C_GRID) 
59:             if ds.is_leave: 
60:                 draw.text((x + 10, y_off + CELL_H), "URL", fill=(200, 0, 0), font=font_b) 
61:                 total_m_leave += emp.daily_hours  # tylko gdy faktycznie urlop 
62:             elif not ds.is_empty(): 
63:                 draw.text((x + 8, y_off + 5), str(ds.start), fill=C_TEXT, font=font_r) 
64:                 draw.text((x + 8, y_off + CELL_H + 5), str(ds.end), fill=C_TEXT, font=font_r) 
65:                 draw.text((x + 12, y_off + 2 * CELL_H + 5), ds.total_as_str(), fill=C_TEXT, font=font_r) 
66:                 total_m_hours += ds.total_duration().total_seconds() / 3600 
67:         y_off += 3 * CELL_H 
68:     # FOOTER 
69:     draw.rectangle([0, y_off, width, y_off + FOOTER_H], fill=C_HEADER_BG, outline=C_GRID, width=1) 
70:     f_labels = [ 
71:         "Godziny pracy", 
72:         "Urlop wypoczynkowy", 
73:         "Inne nieobecności", 
74:         "RAZEM GODZINY" 
75:     ] 
76:     total_hours = int(total_m_hours) 
77:     total_leave = int(total_m_leave) 
78:     f_values = [ 
79:         f"{total_hours}:00", 
80:         f"{total_leave}:00", 
81:         "0:00", 
82:         f"{total_hours + total_leave}:00" 
83:     ] 
84:     val_y = y_off + 20 
85:     for i in range(4): 
86:         draw.text((100, val_y), f_labels[i], fill=C_TEXT, font=font_b) 
87:         draw.text((width // 2, val_y), f_values[i], fill=C_TEXT, font=font_r) 
88:         val_y += 35 
89:     img.save(path, "JPEG", quality=95) 
90:     return True

106:         print("=== START CP-SAT GENERATOR ===") 
107:         self.schedule.clear_unlocked_days()

109:             object.__setattr__(emp, '_orig_daily_hours', emp.daily_hours) 
110:         model = cp_model.CpModel() 
111:         employees = self.schedule.employees 
112:         days = list(range(1, self.schedule.days_in_month + 1)) 
113:         min_open = self.shop.constraints.get("min_open_staff", 3) 
114:         min_close = self.shop.constraints.get("min_close_staff", 3) 
115:         max_consecutive = self.shop.constraints.get("max_consecutive_days", 4) 
116:         trade_days = [d for d in days if self.shop.is_trade_day(d)] 
117:         print("Liczba pracowników:", len(employees)) 
118:         print("Dni w miesiącu:", len(days)) 
119:         print("Dni handlowe:", len(trade_days)) 
120:         print("Min OPEN:", min_open)

122:         print("Max consecutive:", max_consecutive)

300:         all_soft_violations = [] 
301:         all_soft_violations.extend(rest_violations) 
302:         all_soft_violations.extend(balance_violations) 
303:         all_soft_violations.extend(meat_violations) 
304:         all_soft_violations.extend(coverage_violations) 
305:         all_soft_violations.extend(max_consec_violations) 
306:         all_soft_violations.extend(open_violations) 
307:         all_soft_violations.extend(close_violations) 
308:         all_soft_violations.extend(monthly_hours_violations) 
309:         all_soft_violations.extend( 
310:             add_edge_shift_bonus( 
311:                 model, 
312:                 x, 
313:                 employees, 
314:                 trade_days, 
315:                 self.SHIFT_WORK_START_15, 
316:                 self.SHIFT_WORK_END_15 
317:             ) 
318:         )         
319:         all_soft_violations.extend( 
320:             add_morning_afternoon_balance_penalty( 
321:                 model, 
322:                 x, 
323:                 employees, 
324:                 days, 
325:                 self.shop, 
326:                 self.SHIFT_OPEN, 
327:                 self.SHIFT_CLOSE, 
328:                 self.START_SHIFT_MAP, 
329:                 self.END_SHIFT_MAP 
330:             ) 
331:         ) 
332:         all_soft_violations.extend(availability_violations) 
333:         all_soft_violations.extend( 
334:             add_work_balance_penalty( 
335:                 model, 
336:                 x, 
337:                 employees, 
338:                 trade_days, 
339:                 self.START_SHIFT_MAP, 
340:                 self.END_SHIFT_MAP 
341:             ) 
342:         ) 
343:         all_soft_violations.extend( 
344:             add_open_close_penalty( 
345:                 x, 
346:                 employees, 
347:                 trade_days, 
348:                 self.SHIFT_OPEN, 
349:                 self.SHIFT_CLOSE 
350:             ) 
351:         ) 
352:          
353:         build_objective(model, all_soft_violations) 
354:         solver, status = solve_model(model) 
355:         success = save_solution( 
356:             self.schedule, 
357:             self.shop, 
358:             solver, 
359:             status, 
360:             x, 
361:             employees, 
362:             trade_days, 
363:             self.SHIFT_OPEN, 
364:             self.SHIFT_CLOSE, 
365:             self.START_SHIFT_MAP, 
366:             self.END_SHIFT_MAP 
367:         ) 
368:         # SPRZĄTANIE: Przywracamy oryginalne daily_hours, żeby UI i zapisy nie świrowały 
369:         for emp in employees: 
370:             if hasattr(emp, '_orig_daily_hours'): 
371:                 object.__setattr__(emp, 'daily_hours', emp._orig_daily_hours) 
372:         return { 
373:             "status": status, 
374:             "success": success, 
375:             "conflicts": solver.NumConflicts(), 
376:             "branches": solver.NumBranches(), 
377:             "wall_time": solver.WallTime() 
378:         } 
379:      
380:     def _create_variables(self, model, employees, days): 
381:         x = {} 
382:         for e in range(len(employees)): 
383:             for d in days: 
384:                 for s in (self.ALL_SHIFTS): 
385:                     x[e, d, s] = model.NewBoolVar(f"x_e{e}_d{d}_s{s}") 
386:         print(f"[MODEL] variables: {len(x)}") 
387:         return x 
388:      
389:     def _apply_policy( 
390:         self, 
391:         policy_name, 
392:         hard_fn, 
393:         soft_fn=None 
394:     ): 
395:         from model.constraint_policy import ConstraintPolicy 
396:         policy = self.shop.constraint_policies.get(policy_name) 
397:         weight = self.constraint_weights.get(policy_name, 1) 
398:         print(f"[POLICY] {policy_name} -> {policy}") 
399:         if policy == ConstraintPolicy.MANDATORY: 
400:             print(f"[HARD] {policy_name}") 
401:             hard_fn() 
402:             return [] 
403:         elif policy == ConstraintPolicy.PREFERRED: 
404:             print(f"[SOFT] {policy_name} weight={weight}") 
405:             if soft_fn: 
406:                 violations = soft_fn() 
407:                 # zamieniamy violation vars na weighted terms 
408:                 return [weight * v for v in violations] 
409:             else: 
410:                 hard_fn() 
411:                 return [] 
412:         elif policy == ConstraintPolicy.DISABLED: 
413:             return [] 
414:         return []

14:     def get_cell_error(self, emp, day):

18:         return False 
19:     def get_validation_cell_view(self, key, day): 
20:         view = ValidationCellView() 
21:         if not self.shop_config.is_trade_day(day): 
22:             view.bg = theme.BG_DISABLED 
23:             return view 
24:         messages = [] 
25:         for v in self.violations: 
26:             if v.day  
27:                 continue 
28:             if key == "open" and v.type == "min_open_staff": 
29:                 messages.append(v.message) 
30:             elif key == "close" and v.type == "min_close_staff": 
31:                 messages.append(v.message) 
32:             elif key == "meat" and v.type == "meat_coverage": 
33:                 messages.append(v.message) 
34:         if messages: 
35:             view.bg = theme.ERR_RED 
36:             view.tooltip = "\n".join(messages) 
37:         else: 
38:             view.bg = theme.BG_MAIN 
39:         return view

1: class ScheduleController: 
2:     def __init__(self, schedule, shop_config): 
3:         self.schedule = schedule 
4:         self.shop_config = shop_config 
5:         self.history = [] 
6:     def snapshot(self): 
7:         self.history.append(self.schedule.snapshot()) 
8:     def undo(self): 
9:         if not self.history: 
10:             return self.schedule 
11:         self.schedule = self.history.pop() 
12:         return self.schedule 
13:     def set_day_free(self, emp, day): 
14:         self.snapshot() 
15:         self.schedule.set_day_free(emp, day) 
16:         ds = self.schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
17:         ds.is_locked = True 
18:     def set_day_hours(self, emp, day, start, end): 
19:         self.snapshot() 
20:         self.schedule.set_day_hours(emp, day, start, end) 
21:         ds = self.schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
22:         ds.is_locked = True 
23:     def set_day_leave(self, emp, day): 
24:         self.snapshot() 
25:         ds = self.schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
26:         ds.set_leave() 
27:         ds.is_locked = True 
28:     def add_employee(self, emp): 
29:         self.snapshot() 
30:         self.schedule.add_employee(emp) 
31:     def replace_employee(self, old, new): 
32:         self.snapshot() 
33:         self.schedule.replace_employee(old, new) 
34:     def get_day(self, emp, day): 
35:         return self.schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
36:     def generate_schedule(self): 
37:         from logic.auto_generator import AutoScheduleGenerator 
38:         generator = AutoScheduleGenerator(self.schedule, self.shop_config) 
39:         return generator.generate() 
40:     def set_shift(self, emp, day, shift_type, start=None, end=None): 
41:         self.snapshot() 
42:         ds = self.schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
43:         if shift_type == "OFF": 
44:             ds.start = None 
45:             ds.end = None 
46:             ds.is_leave = False 
47:             ds.is_sick = False 
48:         elif shift_type == "LEAVE": 
49:             ds.start = None 
50:             ds.end = None 
51:             ds.is_leave = True 
52:             ds.is_sick = False 
53:         elif shift_type == "WORK": 
54:             if start is not None and end is not None: 
55:                 ds.start = start 
56:                 ds.end = end 
57:             else: 
58:                 hours = self.shop_config.get_open_hours_for_day(day) 
59:                 if hours: 
60:                     ds.start, ds.end = hours 
61:             ds.is_leave = False 
62:             ds.is_sick = False 
63:         ds.is_locked = True 
64:     def _calc_end_from_daily(self, start_str, hours): 
65:         from datetime import datetime, timedelta 
66:         fmt = "%H:%M" 
67:         start = datetime.strptime(start_str, fmt) 
68:         end = start + timedelta(hours=hours) 
69:         return end.strftime(fmt) 
70:      
71:     def remove_employee(self, employee): 
72:         self.schedule.remove_employee(employee) 
73:     def set_day_sick(self, emp, day): 
74:         self.snapshot() 
75:         ds = self.schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
76:         ds.set_sick() 
77:         ds.is_locked = True

1: from dataclasses import dataclass 
2: from ui import theme 
3: @dataclass 
4: class CellView: 
5:     text_start: str = "" 
6:     text_end: str = "" 
7:     text_total: str = "" 
8:     bg: str = theme.BG_MAIN 
9:     tooltip: str | None = None 
10: class SchedulePresenter: 
11:     def __init__(self, schedule, shop_config): 
12:         self.schedule = schedule 
13:         self.shop_config = shop_config 
14:     def get_cell_view(self, emp, day) -> CellView: 
15:         ds = self.schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
16:         s, e, t = ds.as_rows() 
17:         if ds.is_leave: 
18:             return CellView( 
19:                 text_start="🌴", 
20:                 text_end="", 
21:                 text_total="", 
22:                 bg=theme.OK_GREEN, 
23:                 tooltip="Urlop", 
24:             ) 
25:         if not self.shop_config.is_trade_day(day): 
26:             return CellView(bg=theme.BG_DISABLED) 
27:         if not s or not e: 
28:             return CellView(bg=theme.BG_MAIN) 
29:         hours = self.shop_config.get_open_hours_for_day(day) 
30:         text_start = s 
31:         text_end = e 
32:         bg = theme.BG_MAIN 
33:         if hours: 
34:             open_t, close_t = hours 
35:             if s == open_t and emp.daily_hours == 8: 
36:                 text_start = "OTW" 
37:                 text_end = "" 
38:             elif e == close_t and emp.daily_hours == 8: 
39:                 text_start = "ZAM" 
40:                 text_end = "" 
41:             if s == open_t: 
42:                 bg = theme.SHIFT_MORNING 
43:             elif e == close_t: 
44:                 bg = theme.SHIFT_CLOSE 
45:         tooltip = f"{s} - {e}\nSuma: {t}" 
46:         return CellView( 
47:             text_start=text_start, 
48:             text_end=text_end, 
49:             text_total=t, 
50:             bg=bg, 
51:             tooltip=tooltip, 
52:         )

1: from logic.generator.availability_mapper import get_allowed_shifts_for_day 
2: from logic.utils.time_utils import get_effective_daily_hours 
3: def add_availability_constraint( 
4:     model, 
5:     x, 
6:     employees, 
7:     days, 
8:     shop, 
9:     all_shifts, 
10:     SHIFT_OPEN, 
11:     SHIFT_CLOSE, 
12:     START_SHIFT_MAP, 
13:     END_SHIFT_MAP, 
14:     soft=False 
15: ): 
16:     violations = [] 
17:     for e in range(len(employees)): 
18:         emp = employees[e] 
19:         eff_hours = get_effective_daily_hours(emp, shop) 
20:         for d in days: 
21:             if not shop.is_trade_day(d): 
22:                 continue 
23:             allowed = get_allowed_shifts_for_day( 
24:                 emp, 
25:                 d, 
26:                 shop, 
27:                 SHIFT_OPEN, 
28:                 SHIFT_CLOSE, 
29:                 START_SHIFT_MAP, 
30:                 END_SHIFT_MAP 
31:             ) 
32:             # brak ograniczeń → skip 
33:             if allowed is None: 
34:                 continue 
35:             allowed_set = set(allowed) 
36:             # 🔥 NOWE: odrzucamy zmiany które nie mieszczą się w dostępności przy tej długości zmiany 
37:             # (bazujemy na mapperze, ale filtrujemy realnie) 
38:             filtered_allowed = set() 
39:             for s in allowed_set: 
40:                 filtered_allowed.add(s)  # mapper już robi większość roboty 
41:             for s in all_shifts: 
42:                 if s in filtered_allowed: 
43:                     continue 
44:                 if soft: 
45:                     v = model.NewBoolVar(f"avail_violation_e{e}_d{d}_s{s}") 
46:                     model.Add(x[e, d, s] == 1).OnlyEnforceIf(v) 
47:                     violations.append(v) 
48:                 else: 
49:                     model.Add(x[e, d, s] == 0) 
50:     return violations

1: from datetime import datetime, timedelta 
2: def get_effective_daily_hours(emp, shop): 
3:     if emp.employment_fraction == 1.0: 
4:         hours = shop.standard_daily_hours 
5:     else: 
6:         hours = 8.0 
7:     minutes = int(hours * 60) 
8:     minutes = (minutes // 15) * 15 
9:     return minutes / 60 
10: def get_allowed_shifts_for_day( 
11:     emp, 
12:     day, 
13:     shop, 
14:     SHIFT_OPEN, 
15:     SHIFT_CLOSE, 
16:     START_SHIFT_MAP, 
17:     END_SHIFT_MAP 
18: ): 
19:     availability = getattr(emp, "availability", {}) 
20:     weekday = shop.weekday(day) 
21:     rules = availability.get(weekday) 
22:     # brak preferencji → wszystko dozwolone 
23:     if not rules: 
24:         return None 
25:     hours = shop.get_open_hours_for_day(day) 
26:     if not hours: 
27:         return [] 
28:     open_time, close_time = hours 
29:     fmt = "%H:%M" 
30:     open_dt = datetime.strptime(open_time, fmt) 
31:     close_dt = datetime.strptime(close_time, fmt) 
32:     eff_hours = get_effective_daily_hours(emp, shop) 
33:     shift_delta = timedelta(hours=eff_hours) 
34:     allowed = [] 
35:     for rule in rules: 
36:         start_pref = rule["start"] 
37:         end_pref = rule["end"] 
38:         pref_start = datetime.strptime(start_pref, fmt) 
39:         pref_end = datetime.strptime(end_pref, fmt) 
40:         # ===== OPEN ===== 
41:         start = open_dt 
42:         end = start + shift_delta 
43:         if pref_start <= start and end <= pref_end: 
44:             allowed.append(SHIFT_OPEN) 
45:         # ===== CLOSE ===== 
46:         end = close_dt 
47:         start = end - shift_delta 
48:         if pref_start <= start and end <= pref_end: 
49:             allowed.append(SHIFT_CLOSE) 
50:         # ===== START SHIFTS ===== 
51:         for shift, offset in START_SHIFT_MAP.items(): 
52:             start = open_dt + timedelta(minutes=offset) 
53:             end = start + shift_delta 
54:             if pref_start <= start and end <= pref_end: 
55:                 allowed.append(shift) 
56:         # ===== END SHIFTS ===== 
57:         for shift, offset in END_SHIFT_MAP.items(): 
58:             end = close_dt - timedelta(minutes=offset) 
59:             start = end - shift_delta 
60:             if pref_start <= start and end <= pref_end: 
61:                 allowed.append(shift) 
62:     return list(set(allowed))

1: def add_one_shift_per_day_constraint(model, x, employees, days, all_shifts): 
2:     for e in range(len(employees)): 
3:         for d in days: 
4:             model.Add( 
5:                 sum(x[e, d, s] for s in all_shifts) <= 1 
6:             ) 
7: def add_non_trade_day_constraints(model, x, employees, days, shop, all_shifts): 
8:     for e in range(len(employees)): 
9:         for d in days: 
10:             if not shop.is_trade_day(d): 
11:                 for s in all_shifts: 
12:                     model.Add(x[e, d, s] == 0) 
13: def add_leave_constraints(model, x, employees, days, schedule, all_shifts): 
14:     for e in range(len(employees)): 
15:         emp = employees[e] 
16:         for d in days: 
17:             day_state = schedule.get_day(emp, d) 
18:             if day_state.is_leave or day_state.is_sick: 
19:                 for s in all_shifts: 
20:                     model.Add(x[e, d, s] == 0) 
21: def add_day_off_constraints(model, x, employees, days, schedule, all_shifts): 
22:     for e in range(len(employees)): 
23:         emp = employees[e] 
24:         for d in days: 
25:             day_state = schedule.get_day(emp, d) 
26:             if getattr(day_state, "is_day_off", False): 
27:                 for s in all_shifts: 
28:                     model.Add(x[e, d, s] == 0)

1: def add_work_dependency_constraint( 
2:     model, 
3:     x, 
4:     employees, 
5:     days, 
6:     SHIFT_OPEN, 
7:     SHIFT_CLOSE, 
8:     ALL_SHIFTS 
9: ): 
10:     print("[CONSTRAINT] work_dependency") 
11:     for d in days: 
12:         total_open_close = sum( 
13:             x[e, d, SHIFT_OPEN] + x[e, d, SHIFT_CLOSE]

18:                 if s in (SHIFT_OPEN, SHIFT_CLOSE): 
19:                     continue 
20:                 model.Add( 
21:                     x[e, d, s] <= total_open_close 
22:                 )

1: def add_fixed_staff_shift_constraints( 
2:     model, 
3:     x, 
4:     employees, 
5:     trade_days, 
6:     shift_type, 
7:     min_staff, 
8:     soft=False 
9: ): 
10:     print(f"[CONSTRAINT] fixed_staff shift={shift_type} min={min_staff} soft={soft}") 
11:     violations = [] 
12:     for d in trade_days: 
13:         total_staff = sum( 
14:             x[e, d, shift_type] for e in range(len(employees)) 
15:         ) 
16:         opener_staff = sum( 
17:             x[e, d, shift_type] 
18:             for e in range(len(employees)) 
19:             if employees[e].is_opener 
20:         ) 
21:         if not soft: 
22:             meat_staff = sum( 
23:                 x[e, d, shift_type] 
24:                 for e in range(len(employees)) 
25:                 if employees[e].is_meat 
26:             ) 
27:             # Twarde ograniczenia: suma osób musi się zgadzać,  
28:             # ale składy specjalistyczne mogą się nakładać. 
29:             model.Add(total_staff == min_staff) 
30:             model.Add(opener_staff >= 1) 
31:             model.Add(meat_staff >= 1) 
32:         else: 
33:             # Logika soft (kary) jest już poprawnie oparta na >= 1 
34:             total_violation = model.NewIntVar( 
35:                 0, min_staff, 
36:                 f"staff_v_d{d}_{shift_type}" 
37:             ) 
38:             model.Add(total_staff + total_violation >= min_staff) 
39:             violations.append(total_violation) 
40:             opener_violation = model.NewBoolVar( 
41:                 f"opener_v_d{d}_{shift_type}" 
42:             ) 
43:             model.Add(opener_staff + opener_violation >= 1) 
44:             violations.append(opener_violation) 
45:             # Dodajmy mięso do wersji soft, skoro go brakowało 
46:             meat_staff = sum( 
47:                 x[e, d, shift_type] 
48:                 for e in range(len(employees)) 
49:                 if employees[e].is_meat 
50:             ) 
51:             meat_violation = model.NewBoolVar(f"meat_v_d{d}_{shift_type}") 
52:             model.Add(meat_staff + meat_violation >= 1) 
53:             violations.append(meat_violation) 
54:     return violations 
55: def add_max_consecutive_constraint( 
56:     model, 
57:     x, 
58:     employees, 
59:     days, 
60:     max_consecutive, 
61:     all_shifts, 
62:     soft=False 
63: ): 
64:     violations = [] 
65:     for e in range(len(employees)): 
66:         for start in range(1, len(days) - max_consecutive + 1): 
67:             work_sum = sum( 
68:                 x[e, d, s] 
69:                 for d in range(start, start + max_consecutive + 1) 
70:                 for s in all_shifts 
71:             ) 
72:             if not soft: 
73:                 model.Add(work_sum <= max_consecutive) 
74:             else: 
75:                 violation = model.NewIntVar( 
76:                     0, len(days), 
77:                     f"max_consec_violation_e{e}_d{start}" 
78:                 ) 
79:                 model.Add(work_sum <= max_consecutive + violation) 
80:                 violations.append(violation) 
81:     return violations

FILE: C:\Users\kewi1\Desktop\Grafik dino V2\logic\generator\hours_constraint.py

1: from logic.utils.time_utils import get_effective_daily_hours 
2: def add_monthly_hours_constraint( 
3:     model, 
4:     x, 
5:     employees, 
6:     days, 
7:     schedule, 
8:     shop, 
9:     all_shifts, 
10:     soft=False 
11: ): 
12:     violations = [] 
13:     nominal_hours = shop.get_full_time_nominal_hours() 
14:     nominal_minutes = nominal_hours * 60 
15:     all_totals = [] 
16:     for e in range(len(employees)): 
17:         emp = employees[e] 
18:         shift_minutes = int(get_effective_daily_hours(emp, shop) * 60) 
19:         leave_days = 0 
20:         sick_days = 0 
21:         for d in days: 
22:             ds = schedule.get_day(emp, d) 
23:             if ds.is_leave: 
24:                 leave_days += 1 
25:             if getattr(ds, "is_sick", False): 
26:                 sick_days += 1 
27:         leave_minutes = int(leave_days * emp.daily_hours * 60) 
28:         sick_minutes = int(sick_days * emp.daily_hours * 60) 
29:         total_minutes = model.NewIntVar(0, 50000, f"month_total_e{e}") 
30:         model.Add( 
31:             total_minutes == 
32:             sum( 
33:                 x[e, d, s] * shift_minutes 
34:                 for d in days 
35:                 for s in all_shifts 
36:                 if s = 14 
37:             ) 
38:         ) 
39:         all_totals.append(total_minutes) 
40:         target_minutes = int(nominal_minutes * emp.employment_fraction - leave_minutes - sick_minutes) 
41:         if not soft: 
42:             model.Add(total_minutes >= target_minutes) 
43:             model.Add(total_minutes <= target_minutes + (emp.daily_hours * 60)) 
44:         else: 
45:             under = model.NewIntVar(0, 50000, f"under_e{e}") 
46:             model.Add(total_minutes + under >= target_minutes) 
47:             over = model.NewIntVar(0, 50000, f"over_e{e}") 
48:             model.Add(total_minutes <= target_minutes + over) 
49:             violations.append(under) 
50:             violations.append(over) 
51:     if soft and len(all_totals) > 1: 
52:         max_total = model.NewIntVar(0, 50000, "month_max_total") 
53:         min_total = model.NewIntVar(0, 50000, "month_min_total") 
54:         model.AddMaxEquality(max_total, all_totals) 
55:         model.AddMinEquality(min_total, all_totals) 
56:         spread = model.NewIntVar(0, 50000, "month_spread") 
57:         model.Add(spread == max_total - min_total) 
58:         violations.append(spread) 
59:     return violations 
60: def add_balance_constraint( 
61:     model, 
62:     x, 
63:     employees, 
64:     days, 
65:     shop, 
66:     all_shifts, 
67:     soft=True 
68: ): 
69:     nominal = shop.get_full_time_nominal_hours() 
70:     if not nominal: 
71:         return [] 
72:     violations = [] 
73:     for e in range(len(employees)): 
74:         emp = employees[e] 
75:         nominal_minutes = int(nominal * 60 * emp.employment_fraction) 
76:         shift_minutes = int(get_effective_daily_hours(emp, shop) * 60) 
77:         total_minutes = model.NewIntVar(0, 20000, f"total_minutes_e{e}") 
78:         model.Add( 
79:             total_minutes == 
80:             sum( 
81:                 sum(x[e, d, s] for s in all_shifts) * shift_minutes 
82:                 for d in days 
83:             ) 
84:         ) 
85:         if not soft: 
86:             model.Add(total_minutes == nominal_minutes) 
87:         else: 
88:             diff = model.NewIntVar(-20000, 20000, f"diff_e{e}") 
89:             model.Add(diff == total_minutes - nominal_minutes) 
90:             abs_diff = model.NewIntVar(0, 20000, f"abs_diff_e{e}") 
91:             model.AddAbsEquality(abs_diff, diff) 
92:             violations.append(abs_diff) 
93:     return violations

1: from datetime import datetime 
2: def resolve_manual_shift( 
3:     start, 
4:     end, 
5:     open_time, 
6:     close_time, 
7:     start_map, 
8:     end_map 
9: ): 
10:     fmt = "%H:%M" 
11:     if start == open_time: 
12:         return "OPEN" 
13:     if end == close_time: 
14:         return "CLOSE" 
15:     open_dt = datetime.strptime(open_time, fmt) 
16:     start_dt = datetime.strptime(start, fmt) 
17:     diff = int((start_dt - open_dt).total_seconds() / 60) 
18:     if diff in start_map: 
19:         return start_map[diff] 
20:     close_dt = datetime.strptime(close_time, fmt) 
21:     end_dt = datetime.strptime(end, fmt) 
22:     diff = int((close_dt - end_dt).total_seconds() / 60) 
23:     if diff in end_map: 
24:         return end_map[diff] 
25:     return None 
26: def add_manual_shift_constraints( 
27:     model, 
28:     x, 
29:     employees, 
30:     days, 
31:     schedule, 
32:     shop, 
33:     all_shifts, 
34:     SHIFT_OPEN, 
35:     SHIFT_CLOSE, 
36:     START_SHIFT_MAP, 
37:     END_SHIFT_MAP 
38: ): 
39:     for e in range(len(employees)): 
40:         emp = employees[e] 
41:         for d in days: 
42:             day_state = schedule.get_day(emp, d) 
43:             # 🔴 URLop 
44:             if day_state.is_leave: 
45:                 for s in all_shifts: 
46:                     model.Add(x[e, d, s] == 0) 
47:                 continue 
48:             if not day_state.is_locked: 
49:                 continue 
50:             start = getattr(day_state, "start", None) 
51:             end = getattr(day_state, "end", None) 
52:             # 🔴 wolne 
53:             if not start or not end: 
54:                 for s in all_shifts: 
55:                     model.Add(x[e, d, s] == 0) 
56:                 continue 
57:             hours = shop.get_open_hours_for_day(d) 
58:             if not hours: 
59:                 continue 
60:             open_time, close_time = hours 
61:             shift = resolve_manual_shift( 
62:                 start, 
63:                 end, 
64:                 open_time, 
65:                 close_time, 
66:                 {v: k for k, v in START_SHIFT_MAP.items()}, 
67:                 {v: k for k, v in END_SHIFT_MAP.items()} 
68:             ) 
69:             if shift == "OPEN": 
70:                 shift = SHIFT_OPEN 
71:             elif shift == "CLOSE": 
72:                 shift = SHIFT_CLOSE 
73:             if shift is None: 
74:                 continue 
75:             # 🔥 HARD LOCK — solver MUSI to ustawić 
76:             model.Add(x[e, d, shift] == 1) 
77:             for s in all_shifts: 
78:                 if s  
79:                     model.Add(x[e, d, s] == 0)

1: from datetime import datetime, timedelta 
2: from logic.utils.time_utils import get_effective_daily_hours 
3: def add_meat_constraint( 
4:     model, 
5:     x, 
6:     employees, 
7:     days, 
8:     trade_days, 
9:     all_shifts, 
10:     SHIFT_OPEN, 
11:     SHIFT_CLOSE, 
12:     soft=False 
13: ): 
14:     violations = [] 
15:     for d in trade_days: 
16:         meat_on_open = sum( 
17:             x[e, d, SHIFT_OPEN] 
18:             for e in range(len(employees)) 
19:             if employees[e].is_meat 
20:         ) 
21:         meat_on_close = sum( 
22:             x[e, d, SHIFT_CLOSE] 
23:             for e in range(len(employees)) 
24:             if employees[e].is_meat 
25:         ) 
26:         meat_on_work = sum( 
27:             x[e, d, s] 
28:             for e in range(len(employees)) 
29:             for s in all_shifts 
30:             if s not in (SHIFT_OPEN, SHIFT_CLOSE) 
31:             and employees[e].is_meat 
32:         ) 
33:         total_work = sum( 
34:             x[e, d, s] 
35:             for e in range(len(employees)) 
36:             for s in all_shifts 
37:             if s not in (SHIFT_OPEN, SHIFT_CLOSE) 
38:         ) 
39:         if not soft: 
40:             work_exists = model.NewBoolVar(f"work_exists_d{d}") 
41:             model.Add(total_work >= 1).OnlyEnforceIf(work_exists) 
42:             model.Add(total_work == 0).OnlyEnforceIf(work_exists.Not()) 
43:             model.Add( 
44:                 meat_on_work >= 1 
45:             ).OnlyEnforceIf(work_exists) 
46:         else: 
47:             v1 = model.NewBoolVar(f"meat_open_v_d{d}") 
48:             model.Add(meat_on_open + v1 >= 1) 
49:             violations.append(v1) 
50:             v2 = model.NewBoolVar(f"meat_close_v_d{d}") 
51:             model.Add(meat_on_close + v2 >= 1) 
52:             violations.append(v2) 
53:     return violations 
54: def add_meat_coverage_constraint( 
55:     model, 
56:     x, 
57:     employees, 
58:     trade_days, 
59:     shop, 
60:     SHIFT_OPEN, 
61:     SHIFT_CLOSE, 
62:     START_SHIFT_MAP, 
63:     END_SHIFT_MAP, 
64:     soft=False 
65: ): 
66:     violations = [] 
67:     for d in trade_days: 
68:         hours = shop.get_open_hours_for_day(d) 
69:         if not hours: 
70:             continue 
71:         open_time, close_time = hours 
72:         fmt = "%H:%M" 
73:         open_dt = datetime.strptime(open_time, fmt) 
74:         close_dt = datetime.strptime(close_time, fmt) 
75:         t = open_dt 
76:         while t < close_dt: 
77:             slot = t.strftime(fmt) 
78:             meat_cover = [] 
79:             for e in range(len(employees)): 
80:                 if not employees[e].is_meat: 
81:                     continue 
82:                 emp = employees[e] 
83:                 shift_len = timedelta(hours=get_effective_daily_hours(emp, shop)) 
84:                 # OPEN 
85:                 start = open_dt 
86:                 end = start + shift_len 
87:                 if start <= t < end: 
88:                     meat_cover.append(x[e, d, SHIFT_OPEN]) 
89:                 # CLOSE 
90:                 end = close_dt 
91:                 start = end - shift_len 
92:                 if start <= t < end: 
93:                     meat_cover.append(x[e, d, SHIFT_CLOSE]) 
94:                 # WORK od otwarcia 
95:                 for shift, offset in START_SHIFT_MAP.items(): 
96:                     work_start = open_dt + timedelta(minutes=offset) 
97:                     work_end = work_start + shift_len 
98:                     if work_start <= t < work_end: 
99:                         meat_cover.append(x[e, d, shift]) 
100:                 # WORK od zamknięcia 
101:                 for shift, offset in END_SHIFT_MAP.items(): 
102:                     work_end = close_dt - timedelta(minutes=offset) 
103:                     work_start = work_end - shift_len 
104:                     if work_start <= t < work_end: 
105:                         meat_cover.append(x[e, d, shift]) 
106:             if not meat_cover: 
107:                 t += timedelta(minutes=15) 
108:                 continue 
109:             if not soft: 
110:                 model.Add(sum(meat_cover) >= 1) 
111:             else: 
112:                 v = model.NewBoolVar(f"meat_cover_v_d{d}_{slot}") 
113:                 model.Add(sum(meat_cover) + v >= 1) 
114:                 violations.append(v) 
115:             t += timedelta(minutes=15) 
116:     return violations

36: def add_morning_afternoon_balance_penalty( 
37:     model, 
38:     x, 
39:     employees, 
40:     days, 
41:     shop, # Zostawiam dla zachowania sygnatury, choć w tej logice nie jest używane 
42:     SHIFT_OPEN, 
43:     SHIFT_CLOSE, 
44:     START_SHIFT_MAP, 
45:     END_SHIFT_MAP 
46: ): 
47:     print("[OBJECTIVE] balance daily Morning vs Afternoon staff") 
48:     penalties = [] 
49:     # Iterujemy po dniach, a nie po pracownikach 
50:     for d in days: 
51:          
52:         # Sumujemy wszystkie poranne zmiany (Otwarcie + przesunięcia od otwarcia) w danym dniu 
53:         morning_shifts = sum( 
54:             x[e, d, s] 
55:             for e in range(len(employees)) 
56:             for s in [SHIFT_OPEN] + list(START_SHIFT_MAP.keys()) 
57:         ) 
58:         # Sumujemy wszystkie popołudniowe zmiany (Zamknięcie + przesunięcia do zamknięcia) w danym dniu 
59:         afternoon_shifts = sum( 
60:             x[e, d, s] 
61:             for e in range(len(employees)) 
62:             for s in [SHIFT_CLOSE] + list(END_SHIFT_MAP.keys()) 
63:         ) 
64:         # Obliczamy różnicę między rano a popo 
65:         diff = model.NewIntVar(-50, 50, f"daily_balance_diff_d{d}") 
66:         model.Add(diff == morning_shifts - afternoon_shifts) 
67:         # Pobieramy wartość absolutną różnicy (aby karać za odchylenia w obie strony) 
68:         abs_diff = model.NewIntVar(0, 50, f"daily_balance_abs_d{d}") 
69:         model.AddAbsEquality(abs_diff, diff) 
70:         # Dodajemy różnicę do ogólnej puli kar (im większa różnica, tym gorzej) 
71:         penalties.append(abs_diff) 
72:     return penalties 
73: def add_edge_shift_bonus( 
74:     model, 
75:     x, 
76:     employees, 
77:     days, 
78:     SHIFT_WORK_START_15, 
79:     SHIFT_WORK_END_15 
80: ): 
81:     penalties = [] 
82:     for d in days: 
83:         start_15_exists = model.NewBoolVar(f"start15_exists_d{d}") 
84:         end_15_exists = model.NewBoolVar(f"end15_exists_d{d}")

86:         model.Add( 
87:             sum(x[e, d, SHIFT_WORK_START_15] for e in range(len(employees))) >= 1 
88:         ).OnlyEnforceIf(start_15_exists) 
89:         model.Add( 
90:             sum(x[e, d, SHIFT_WORK_START_15] for e in range(len(employees))) == 0 
91:         ).OnlyEnforceIf(start_15_exists.Not()) 
92:         # czy ktoś ma -15 od zamknięcia 
93:         model.Add( 
94:             sum(x[e, d, SHIFT_WORK_END_15] for e in range(len(employees))) >= 1 
95:         ).OnlyEnforceIf(end_15_exists) 
96:         model.Add( 
97:             sum(x[e, d, SHIFT_WORK_END_15] for e in range(len(employees))) == 0 
98:         ).OnlyEnforceIf(end_15_exists.Not()) 
99:         # kara jeśli brak 
100:         penalties.append(start_15_exists.Not()) 
101:         penalties.append(end_15_exists.Not()) 
102:     return penalties

1: from ortools.sat.python import cp_model 
2: from datetime import datetime, timedelta 
3: from model.day_schedule import calc_start, calc_end 
4: from logic.utils.time_utils import get_effective_daily_hours 
5: def add_rest_11h_constraint( 
6:     model, 
7:     x, 
8:     employees, 
9:     days, 
10:     trade_days, 
11:     shop, 
12:     SHIFT_OPEN, 
13:     SHIFT_CLOSE, 
14:     START_SHIFTS, 
15:     END_SHIFTS, 
16:     soft=False 
17: ): 
18:     fmt = "%H:%M" 
19:     violations = [] 
20:     rest_constraints = 0 
21:     for e in range(len(employees)): 
22:         emp = employees[e] 
23:         eff_hours = get_effective_daily_hours(emp, shop) 
24:         for i in range(len(days) - 1): 
25:             d = days[i] 
26:             d_next = days[i + 1] 
27:             if d not in trade_days or d_next not in trade_days: 
28:                 continue 
29:             hours_d = shop.get_open_hours_for_day(d) 
30:             hours_next = shop.get_open_hours_for_day(d_next) 
31:             if not hours_d or not hours_next: 
32:                 continue 
33:             open_d, close_d = hours_d 
34:             open_next, close_next = hours_next 
35:             shifts_today = {} 
36:             shifts_today[SHIFT_OPEN] = ( 
37:                 open_d, 
38:                 calc_end(open_d, eff_hours) 
39:             ) 
40:             shifts_today[SHIFT_CLOSE] = ( 
41:                 calc_start(close_d, eff_hours), 
42:                 close_d 
43:             ) 
44:             for shift, off in START_SHIFTS.items(): 
45:                 start = ( 
46:                     datetime.strptime(open_d, fmt) 
47:                     + timedelta(minutes=off) 
48:                 ).strftime(fmt) 
49:                 shifts_today[shift] = ( 
50:                     start, 
51:                     calc_end(start, eff_hours) 
52:                 ) 
53:             for shift, off in END_SHIFTS.items(): 
54:                 end = ( 
55:                     datetime.strptime(close_d, fmt) 
56:                     - timedelta(minutes=off) 
57:                 ).strftime(fmt) 
58:                 shifts_today[shift] = ( 
59:                     calc_start(end, eff_hours), 
60:                     end 
61:                 ) 
62:             shifts_next = {} 
63:             shifts_next[SHIFT_OPEN] = ( 
64:                 open_next, 
65:                 calc_end(open_next, eff_hours) 
66:             ) 
67:             shifts_next[SHIFT_CLOSE] = ( 
68:                 calc_start(close_next, eff_hours), 
69:                 close_next 
70:             ) 
71:             for shift, off in START_SHIFTS.items(): 
72:                 start = ( 
73:                     datetime.strptime(open_next, fmt) 
74:                     + timedelta(minutes=off) 
75:                 ).strftime(fmt) 
76:                 shifts_next[shift] = ( 
77:                     start, 
78:                     calc_end(start, eff_hours) 
79:                 ) 
80:             for shift, off in END_SHIFTS.items(): 
81:                 end = ( 
82:                     datetime.strptime(close_next, fmt) 
83:                     - timedelta(minutes=off) 
84:                 ).strftime(fmt) 
85:                 shifts_next[shift] = ( 
86:                     calc_start(end, eff_hours), 
87:                     end 
88:                 ) 
89:             for s1 in shifts_today: 
90:                 for s2 in shifts_next: 
91:                     end_today = datetime.strptime(shifts_today[s1][1], fmt) 
92:                     start_next = datetime.strptime(shifts_next[s2][0], fmt) 
93:                     rest = start_next - end_today 
94:                     if rest.total_seconds() < 0: 
95:                         rest += timedelta(days=1) 
96:                     if rest < timedelta(hours=11): 
97:                         if not soft: 
98:                             model.Add( 
99:                                 x[e, d, s1] + x[e, d_next, s2] <= 1 
100:                             ) 
101:                         else: 
102:                             violation = model.NewBoolVar( 
103:                                 f"rest_violation_e{e}_d{d}_{s1}_{s2}" 
104:                             ) 
105:                             model.Add( 
106:                                 x[e, d, s1] + x[e, d_next, s2] <= 1 + violation 
107:                             ) 
108:                             violations.append(violation) 
109:                         rest_constraints += 1 
110:     print("Constrainty 11h rest:", rest_constraints) 
111:     return violations

1: from ortools.sat.python import cp_model 
2: from datetime import datetime, timedelta 
3: from model.day_schedule import calc_start, calc_end 
4: from logic.utils.time_utils import get_effective_daily_hours 
5: def save_solution( 
6:     schedule, 
7:     shop, 
8:     solver, 
9:     status, 
10:     x, 
11:     employees, 
12:     trade_days, 
13:     SHIFT_OPEN, 
14:     SHIFT_CLOSE, 
15:     START_SHIFTS, 
16:     END_SHIFTS 
17: ): 
18:     if status not in (cp_model.OPTIMAL, cp_model.FEASIBLE): 
19:         print("❌ BRAK ROZWIĄZANIA") 
20:         return False 
21:     print("✅ ROZWIĄZANIE ZNALEZIONE") 
22:     print("=== PODSUMOWANIE ZMIAN ===") 
23:     for d in trade_days: 
24:         open_count = sum( 
25:             solver.Value(x[e, d, SHIFT_OPEN]) 
26:             for e in range(len(employees)) 
27:         ) 
28:         close_count = sum( 
29:             solver.Value(x[e, d, SHIFT_CLOSE]) 
30:             for e in range(len(employees)) 
31:         ) 
32:         work_count = sum( 
33:             solver.Value(x[e, d, s]) 
34:             for e in range(len(employees)) 
35:             for s in list(START_SHIFTS.keys()) + list(END_SHIFTS.keys()) 
36:         ) 
37:         print(f"Dzień {d}: OPEN={open_count} CLOSE={close_count} WORK={work_count}") 
38:     for e in range(len(employees)): 
39:         emp = employees[e] 
40:         for d in trade_days: 
41:             day_state = schedule.get_day(emp, d) 
42:             if ( 
43:                 day_state.is_leave 
44:                 or day_state.is_locked 
45:                 or getattr(day_state, "is_day_off", False) 
46:             ): 
47:                 continue 
48:             hours = shop.get_open_hours_for_day(d) 
49:             if not hours: 
50:                 continue 
51:             open_time, close_time = hours 
52:             fmt = "%H:%M" 
53:             eff_hours = get_effective_daily_hours(emp, shop) 
54:             if solver.Value(x[e, d, SHIFT_OPEN]) == 1: 
55:                 end = calc_end(open_time, eff_hours) 
56:                 schedule.set_day_hours(emp, d, open_time, end) 
57:                 continue 
58:             if solver.Value(x[e, d, SHIFT_CLOSE]) == 1: 
59:                 start = calc_start(close_time, eff_hours) 
60:                 schedule.set_day_hours(emp, d, start, close_time) 
61:                 continue 
62:             assigned = False 
63:             for shift, offset in START_SHIFTS.items(): 
64:                 if solver.Value(x[e, d, shift]) == 1: 
65:                     start_dt = datetime.strptime(open_time, fmt) + timedelta(minutes=offset) 
66:                     start = start_dt.strftime(fmt) 
67:                     end = calc_end(start, eff_hours) 
68:                     schedule.set_day_hours(emp, d, start, end) 
69:                     assigned = True 
70:                     break 
71:             if not assigned: 
72:                 for shift, offset in END_SHIFTS.items(): 
73:                     if solver.Value(x[e, d, shift]) == 1: 
74:                         end_dt = datetime.strptime(close_time, fmt) - timedelta(minutes=offset) 
75:                         end = end_dt.strftime(fmt) 
76:                         start = calc_start(end, eff_hours) 
77:                         schedule.set_day_hours(emp, d, start, end) 
78:                         break 
79:     print("=== KONIEC GENERATORA ===") 
80:     return True

1: from ortools.sat.python import cp_model 
2: def build_objective(model, weighted_soft_terms): 
3:     if weighted_soft_terms: 
4:         print("[OBJECTIVE] terms:", len(weighted_soft_terms)) 
5:         model.Maximize(-sum(weighted_soft_terms)) 
6: def solve_model(model): 
7:     solver = cp_model.CpSolver() 
8:     solver.parameters.max_time_in_seconds = 60 
9:     solver.parameters.num_search_workers = 10 
10:     status = solver.Solve(model) 
11:     print("Status:", solver.StatusName(status)) 
12:     print("Czas:", solver.WallTime(), "s") 
13:     print("Conflicts:", solver.NumConflicts()) 
14:     print("Branches:", solver.NumBranches()) 
15:     return solver, status

1: def get_effective_daily_hours(emp, shop): 
2:     # 🔴 tylko full-time dostaje 8:45 
3:     if shop.constraints.get("force_fulltime_845", False) and emp.employment_fraction == 1.0: 
4:         hours = 8.75 
5:     else: 
6:         # 🔴 zawsze bazujemy na 8h dla ułamków 
7:         hours = 8.0 * emp.employment_fraction 
8:     minutes = int(hours * 60) 
9:     minutes = (minutes // 15) * 15 
10:     return minutes / 60

1: from dataclasses import dataclass 
2: from typing import List 
3: from model.month_schedule import MonthSchedule 
4: from model.shop_config import ShopConfig 
5: from model.constraint_policy import ConstraintPolicy 
6: # ========================================== 
7: # RESULT 
8: # ========================================== 
9: @dataclass 
10: class ConstraintViolation: 
11:     type: str          # np. "max_consecutive_days" 
12:     employee: object   # Employee lub None (jeśli globalne) 
13:     day: int | None 
14:     message: str 
15: # ========================================== 
16: # ENGINE 
17: # ========================================== 
18: # ========================================== 
19: # RULE BASE 
20: # ========================================== 
21: class Rule: 
22:     def apply(self, schedule: MonthSchedule, shop: ShopConfig) -> List[ConstraintViolation]: 
23:         raise NotImplementedError 
24: # ========================================== 
25: # RULES 
26: # ========================================== 
27: class MaxConsecutiveDaysRule(Rule): 
28:     def __init__(self, limit: int): 
29:         self.limit = limit 
30:     def apply(self, schedule, shop): 
31:         results = [] 
32:         for emp in schedule.employees: 
33:             streak = 0 
34:             for day in range(1, schedule.days_in_month + 1): 
35:                 ds = schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
36:                 if not ds.is_empty(): 
37:                     streak += 1 
38:                 else: 
39:                     streak = 0 
40:                 if streak > self.limit: 
41:                     results.append( 
42:                         ConstraintViolation( 
43:                             type="max_consecutive_days", 
44:                             employee=emp, 
45:                             day=day, 
46:                             message=f"Więcej niż {self.limit} dni pracy pod rząd" 
47:                         ) 
48:                     ) 
49:         return results 
50: class MinStaffRule(Rule): 
51:     def __init__(self, minimum: int, mode: str): 
52:         self.minimum = minimum 
53:         self.mode = mode  # "open" | "close" 
54:     def apply(self, schedule, shop): 
55:         results = [] 
56:         for day in range(1, schedule.days_in_month + 1): 
57:             stats = opening_closing_stats(schedule, shop, day, self.mode) 
58:             if stats["count"] < self.minimum: 
59:                 results.append( 
60:                     ConstraintViolation( 
61:                         type=f"min_{self.mode}_staff", 
62:                         employee=None, 
63:                         day=day, 
64:                         message=( 
65:                             f"Za mało osób na " 
66:                             f"{'otwarciu' if self.mode == 'open' else 'zamknięciu'} " 
67:                             f"(min {self.minimum})" 
68:                         ) 
69:                     ) 
70:                 ) 
71:         return results 
72: class Rest11hRule(Rule): 
73:     def apply(self, schedule, shop): 
74:         from datetime import datetime, timedelta 
75:         results = [] 
76:         fmt = "%H:%M" 
77:         for emp in schedule.employees: 
78:             for day in range(1, schedule.days_in_month): 
79:                 today = schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
80:                 next_day = schedule.get_day(emp, day + 1) 
81:                 if today.is_empty() or next_day.is_empty(): 
82:                     continue 
83:                 end_today = datetime.strptime(today.end, fmt) 
84:                 start_next = datetime.strptime(next_day.start, fmt) 
85:                 start_next += timedelta(days=1) 
86:                 rest = start_next - end_today 
87:                 hours = rest.total_seconds() / 3600 
88:                 if hours < 11: 
89:                     results.append( 
90:                         ConstraintViolation( 
91:                             type="rest_11h", 
92:                             employee=emp, 
93:                             day=day + 1, 
94:                             message=f"Przerwa tylko {round(hours,2)}h (min 11h)" 
95:                         ) 
96:                     ) 
97:         return results 
98: class MeatCoverageRule(Rule): 
99:     def apply(self, schedule, shop): 
100:         results = [] 
101:         for day in range(1, schedule.days_in_month + 1): 
102:             result = meat_coverage(schedule, shop, day) 
103:             if not result["ok"]: 
104:                 if result["gap"] is None: 
105:                     msg = "Brak mięsa przez cały dzień" 
106:                 else: 
107:                     start, end = result["gap"] 
108:                     msg = f"Brak mięsa od {start} do {end}" 
109:                 results.append( 
110:                     ConstraintViolation( 
111:                         type="meat_coverage", 
112:                         employee=None, 
113:                         day=day, 
114:                         message=msg 
115:                     ) 
116:                 ) 
117:         return results 
118: # ========================================== 
119: # ENGINE 
120: # ========================================== 
121: class ConstraintEngine: 
122:     @staticmethod 
123:     def evaluate(schedule: MonthSchedule, 
124:                  shop: ShopConfig) -> List[ConstraintViolation]: 
125:         cfg = shop.constraints 
126:         rules: List[Rule] = [] 
127:         if "max_consecutive_days" in cfg: 
128:             rules.append( 
129:                 MaxConsecutiveDaysRule(cfg["max_consecutive_days"]) 
130:             ) 
131:         if "min_open_staff" in cfg: 
132:             rules.append( 
133:                 MinStaffRule(cfg["min_open_staff"], "open") 
134:             ) 
135:         if "min_close_staff" in cfg: 
136:             rules.append( 
137:                 MinStaffRule(cfg["min_close_staff"], "close") 
138:             ) 
139:         if cfg.get("enforce_11h_rest", False): 
140:             rules.append(Rest11hRule()) 
141:         meat_policy = shop.constraint_policies.get("meat_coverage", ConstraintPolicy.MANDATORY) 
142:         if meat_policy  
143:             rules.append(MeatCoverageRule()) 
144:         violations: List[ConstraintViolation] = [] 
145:         for rule in rules: 
146:             violations.extend(rule.apply(schedule, shop)) 
147:         return violations 
148: def opening_closing_stats( 
149:     schedule: MonthSchedule, 
150:     shop: ShopConfig, 
151:     day: int, 
152:     mode: str  # "open" | "close" 
153: ) -> dict: 
154:     open_hours = shop.get_open_hours_for_day(day) 
155:     if not open_hours: 
156:         return {"count": 0, "has_opener": False} 
157:     target_time = open_hours[0] if mode == "open" else open_hours[1] 
158:     count = 0 
159:     has_opener = False 
160:     for emp in schedule.employees: 
161:         ds = schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
162:         if ds.is_empty(): 
163:             continue 
164:         time = ds.start if mode == "open" else ds.end 
165:         if time == target_time: 
166:             count += 1 
167:             if emp.is_opener: 
168:                 has_opener = True 
169:     return {"count": count, "has_opener": has_opener} 
170: # ================================================== 
171: # MIĘSO 
172: # ================================================== 
173: from datetime import datetime 
174: FMT = "%H:%M" 
175: def meat_coverage(schedule, shop, day: int) -> dict: 
176:     """ 
177:     Sprawdza czy mięso jest pokryte przez cały dzień. 
178:     Wersja zoptymalizowana – analiza przedziałowa. 
179:     """ 
180:     open_hours = shop.get_open_hours_for_day(day) 
181:     if not open_hours: 
182:         return {"ok": True, "gap": None} 
183:     open_t = datetime.strptime(open_hours[0], FMT) 
184:     close_t = datetime.strptime(open_hours[1], FMT) 
185:     intervals = [] 
186:     # 🔹 zbierz przedziały tylko dla pracowników z mięsem 
187:     for emp in schedule.employees: 
188:         if not emp.is_meat: 
189:             continue 
190:         ds = schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
191:         if ds.is_empty(): 
192:             continue 
193:         start = datetime.strptime(ds.start, FMT) 
194:         end = datetime.strptime(ds.end, FMT) 
195:         # ignorujemy błędne zakresy 
196:         if start >= end: 
197:             continue 
198:         intervals.append((start, end)) 
199:     if not intervals: 
200:         return { 
201:             "ok": False, 
202:             "gap": (open_t.strftime(FMT), close_t.strftime(FMT)) 
203:         } 
204:     # 🔹 sortujemy po czasie rozpoczęcia 
205:     intervals.sort(key=lambda x: x[0]) 
206:     current = open_t 
207:     for start, end in intervals: 
208:         # luka przed kolejnym przedziałem 
209:         if start > current: 
210:             return { 
211:                 "ok": False, 
212:                 "gap": (current.strftime(FMT), start.strftime(FMT)) 
213:             } 
214:         # rozszerzamy pokrycie 
215:         if end > current: 
216:             current = end 
217:         if current >= close_t: 
218:             return {"ok": True, "gap": None} 
219:     # jeśli po przejściu wszystkich nadal nie pokryliśmy 
220:     if current < close_t: 
221:         return { 
222:             "ok": False, 
223:             "gap": (current.strftime(FMT), close_t.strftime(FMT)) 
224:         } 
225:     return {"ok": True, "gap": None} 
226: def rest_11h_violation(schedule: MonthSchedule, emp, day: int): 
227:     """ 
228:     Zwraca: 
229:     { 
230:         "violation": bool, 
231:         "rest_hours": float | None 
232:     } 
233:     """ 
234:     if day < 1 or day >= schedule.days_in_month: 
235:         return {"violation": False, "rest_hours": None} 
236:     today = schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
237:     next_day = schedule.get_day(emp, day + 1) 
238:     if today.is_empty() or next_day.is_empty(): 
239:         return {"violation": False, "rest_hours": None} 
240:     from datetime import datetime, timedelta 
241:     fmt = "%H:%M" 
242:     end_today = datetime.strptime(today.end, fmt) 
243:     start_next = datetime.strptime(next_day.start, fmt) 
244:     # 🔥 uwzględnij przejście do kolejnego dnia 
245:     start_next += timedelta(days=1) 
246:     rest = start_next - end_today 
247:     hours = rest.total_seconds() / 3600 
248:     return { 
249:         "violation": hours < 11, 
250:         "rest_hours": round(hours, 2) 
251:     }

5:     DISABLED = "DISABLED"       # wyłączony

1: from dataclasses import dataclass 
2: from datetime import datetime, timedelta 
3: _TIME_FORMAT = "%H:%M" 
4: def _parse_time(value: str) -> datetime: 
5:     return datetime.strptime(value, _TIME_FORMAT) 
6: @dataclass 
7: class DaySchedule: 
8:     """ 
9:     Jedna komórka grafiku (jeden dzień, jeden pracownik). 
10:     Przechowuje: 
11:     - start pracy 
12:     - koniec pracy 
13:     - flagę urlopu 
14:     """ 
15:     start: str | None = None 
16:     end: str | None = None 
17:     is_leave: bool = False   # ← DODANE 
18:     is_locked: bool = False 
19:     is_sick: bool = False 
20:     def is_empty(self) -> bool: 
21:         """Czy dzień jest pusty (wolne).""" 
22:         return self.start is None and self.end is None 
23:     def set_free(self) -> None: 
24:         """Ustawia dzień jako wolny.""" 
25:         self.start = None 
26:         self.end = None 
27:         self.is_leave = False 
28:         self.is_sick = False 
29:     def set_leave(self) -> None: 
30:         """Ustawia dzień jako urlop.""" 
31:         self.start = None 
32:         self.end = None 
33:         self.is_leave = True 
34:         self.is_sick = False   
35:     def set_hours(self, start: str, end: str) -> None: 
36:         """ 
37:         Ustawia godziny pracy. 
38:         Format: 'HH:MM' 
39:         """ 
40:         start_dt = _parse_time(start) 
41:         end_dt = _parse_time(end) 
42:         if end_dt <= start_dt: 
43:             raise ValueError("Godzina zakończenia musi być późniejsza niż rozpoczęcia") 
44:         self.start = start 
45:         self.end = end 
46:         self.is_leave = False 
47:         self.is_sick = False 
48:     def total_duration(self) -> timedelta | None: 
49:         """ 
50:         Zwraca czas pracy jako timedelta. 
51:         """ 
52:         if self.is_empty() or self.is_leave or self.is_sick: 
53:             return None 
54:         start_dt = _parse_time(self.start) 
55:         end_dt = _parse_time(self.end) 
56:         return end_dt - start_dt 
57:     def total_as_str(self) -> str | None: 
58:         """ 
59:         Zwraca sumę godzin w formacie HH:MM. 
60:         """ 
61:         duration = self.total_duration() 
62:         if duration is None: 
63:             return None 
64:         total_minutes = int(duration.total_seconds() // 60) 
65:         hours = total_minutes // 60 
66:         minutes = total_minutes % 60 
67:         return f"{hours}:{minutes:02d}" 
68:     def as_rows(self) -> tuple[str, str, str]: 
69:         """ 
70:         Zwraca dane dokładnie pod GUI: 
71:         (start, end, suma) 
72:         Jeśli wolne → puste stringi 
73:         Jeśli urlop → 🌴 w pierwszej linii 
74:         """ 
75:         if self.is_leave: 
76:             return "🌴", "", "" 
77:         if self.is_sick: 
78:             return "🤒", "", "" 
79:         if self.is_empty(): 
80:             return "", "", "" 
81:         return ( 
82:             self.start or "", 
83:             self.end or "", 
84:             self.total_as_str() or "", 
85:         ) 
86:     def set_sick(self): 
87:         self.start = None 
88:         self.end = None 
89:         self.is_leave = False 
90:         self.is_sick = True 
91:     def total_minutes(self) -> int: 
92:         """ 
93:         Zwraca czas pracy w minutach (int). 
94:         Jeśli brak pracy → 0. 
95:         """ 
96:         duration = self.total_duration() 
97:         if duration is None: 
98:             return 0 
99:         return int(duration.total_seconds() // 60) 
100: def calc_end(start_str: str, hours: float) -> str: 
101:     fmt = "%H:%M" 
102:     start = datetime.strptime(start_str, fmt) 
103:     end = start + timedelta(hours=hours) 
104:     return end.strftime(fmt) 
105: def calc_start(end_str: str, hours: float) -> str: 
106:     fmt = "%H:%M" 
107:     end = datetime.strptime(end_str, fmt) 
108:     start = end - timedelta(hours=hours) 
109:     return start.strftime(fmt)

7:     Reprezentuje jednego pracownika. 
8:     frozen=True: 
9:     - obiekt jest hashowalny 
10:     - może być bezpiecznie używany jako klucz w dict 
11:     """

13:     last_name: str 
14:     first_name: str 
15:     # pozostałe dane (nie wpływają na sortowanie) 
16:     is_opener: bool = field(default=False, compare=False) 
17:     is_meat: bool = field(default=False, compare=False) 
18:     monthly_target_hours: int = field(default=160, compare=False) 
19:     daily_hours: int = field(default=8, compare=False) 
20:     # 🔥 NOWE POLE 
21:     employment_fraction: float = field(default=1.0, compare=False) 
22:     id: str = field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()), compare=False) 
23:     availability: Dict[int, dict] = field(default_factory=dict, compare=False)

25:         return f"{self.last_name} {self.first_name}" 
26:     def validate(self) -> None: 
27:         if not self.last_name.strip(): 
28:             raise ValueError("Nazwisko nie może być puste") 
29:         if not self.first_name.strip(): 
30:             raise ValueError("Imię nie może być puste") 
31:         # 🔧 ZMIANA – luzujemy ograniczenie 
32:         if self.daily_hours <= 0: 
33:             raise ValueError("Dzienna liczba godzin musi być większa od 0") 
34:         # 🔥 NOWA WALIDACJA 
35:         if self.employment_fraction <= 0 or self.employment_fraction > 1: 
36:             raise ValueError("Wymiar etatu musi być w zakresie (0, 1]") 
37:         for wd, cfg in self.availability.items(): 
38:             if wd < 0 or wd > 6: 
39:                 raise ValueError("Nieprawidłowy dzień tygodnia") 
40:             if "start" not in cfg or "end" not in cfg: 
41:                 raise ValueError("Brak godzin w availability") 
42:             if cfg.get("mode") not in ("hard", "soft"): 
43:                 raise ValueError("Nieprawidłowy tryb availability")

169:         if old not in self._data: 
170:             return 
171:         days_data = self._data[old] 
172:         self.remove_employee(old) 
173:         self.add_employee(new) 
174:         self._data[new] = days_data 
175:     def clear_unlocked_days(self): 
176:         for emp in self.employees: 
177:             for d in range(1, self.days_in_month + 1): 
178:                 day_data = self.get_day(emp, d) 
179:                 if not day_data.is_locked: 
180:                     day_data.start = None 
181:                     day_data.end = None 
182:                     if hasattr(day_data, "is_day_off"): 
183:                         day_data.is_day_off = False

FILE: C:\Users\kewi1\Desktop\Grafik dino V2\model\shop_config.py 
================================================== 
 
1: import calendar 
2: from model.constraint_policy import ConstraintPolicy 
3: class ShopConfig: 
4:     """ 
5:     Konfiguracja sklepu: 
6:     - niedziele handlowe 
7:     - godziny otwarcia per dzień tygodnia 
8:     - constrainty 
9:     - opcje UI 
10:     """ 
11:     def __init__(self, year: int, month: int): 
12:         self.year = year 
13:         self.month = month 
14:         # Toggle dla constraintów z model.constraint_policy 
15:         self.constraint_policies = { 
16:             "rest_11h": ConstraintPolicy.MANDATORY, 
17:             "meat": ConstraintPolicy.PREFERRED, 
18:             "balance": ConstraintPolicy.PREFERRED, 
19:             "max_consecutive": ConstraintPolicy.PREFERRED, 
20:             "open": ConstraintPolicy.MANDATORY, 
21:             "close": ConstraintPolicy.MANDATORY, 
22:             "monthly_hours": ConstraintPolicy.PREFERRED, 
23:             "meat_coverage": ConstraintPolicy.PREFERRED, 
24:             "availability": ConstraintPolicy.MANDATORY, 
25:         } 
26:         # ----------------------------- 
27:         # Override godzin dla konkretnego dnia 
28:         # ----------------------------- 
29:         self.day_overrides: dict[int, tuple[str, str]] = {} 
30:         # ----------------------------- 
31:         # CONSTRAINTS CONFIG 
32:         # ----------------------------- 
33:         self.constraints = { 
34:             "max_consecutive_days": 4, 
35:             "min_open_staff": 3, 
36:             "min_close_staff": 3, 
37:         } 
38:         # ----------------------------- 
39:         # UI OPTIONS 
40:         # ----------------------------- 
41:         # "compact" | "detailed" 
42:         self.cell_display_mode = "compact" 
43:         # ----------------------------- 
44:         # Niedziele handlowe 
45:         # ----------------------------- 
46:         self.trade_sundays: set[int] = set() 
47:         # dni ustawowo wolne 
48:         self.public_holidays: set[int] = set() 
49:         self.standard_daily_hours = 8.0 
50:         # ----------------------------- 
51:         # Godziny otwarcia per weekday 
52:         # (0=Pn ... 6=Nd) 
53:         # ----------------------------- 
54:         self.open_hours: dict[int, tuple[str, str]] = { 
55:             0: ("05:30", "22:45"), 
56:             1: ("05:30", "22:45"), 
57:             2: ("05:30", "22:45"), 
58:             3: ("05:30", "22:45"), 
59:             4: ("05:30", "22:45"), 
60:             5: ("05:30", "22:45"), 
61:             6: ("05:30", "22:45"),  # Nd (jeśli handlowa) 
62:         } 
63:     # ========================================================== 
64:     # PODSTAWOWE METODY 
65:     # ========================================================== 
66:     def weekday(self, day: int) -> int: 
67:         return calendar.weekday(self.year, self.month, day) 
68:     def is_sunday(self, day: int) -> bool: 
69:         return self.weekday(day) == 6 
70:     def is_trade_day(self, day: int) -> bool: 
71:         if day in self.public_holidays: 
72:             return False 
73:         if self.is_sunday(day): 
74:             return day in self.trade_sundays 
75:         return True 
76:     # ========================================================== 
77:     # GODZINY OTWARCIA 
78:     # ========================================================== 
79:     def get_open_hours_for_day(self, day: int) -> tuple[str, str] | None: 
80:         """ 
81:         Zwraca (open, close) albo None jeśli sklep zamknięty 
82:         lub brak poprawnych godzin. 
83:         """ 
84:         if not self.is_trade_day(day): 
85:             return None 
86:         # override ma najwyższy priorytet 
87:         if day in self.day_overrides: 
88:             start, end = self.day_overrides[day] 
89:             if start and end: 
90:                 return start, end 
91:             return None 
92:         wd = self.weekday(day) 
93:         hours = self.open_hours.get(wd) 
94:         if not hours: 
95:             return None 
96:         start, end = hours 
97:         if not start or not end: 
98:             return None 
99:         return start, end 
100:     def get_open_hours_for_weekday(self, weekday: int) -> tuple[str, str]: 
101:         return self.open_hours[weekday] 
102:     def set_open_hours_for_weekday(self, weekday: int, start: str, end: str): 
103:         self.open_hours[weekday] = (start, end) 
104:     # ========================================================== 
105:     # SERIALIZACJA 
106:     # ========================================================== 
107:     def to_dict(self): 
108:         return { 
109:             "year": self.year, 
110:             "month": self.month, 
111:             "open_hours": self.open_hours, 
112:             "trade_sundays": list(self.trade_sundays), 
113:             "day_overrides": self.day_overrides, 
114:             "constraints": self.constraints, 
115:             "cell_display_mode": self.cell_display_mode, 
116:             "public_holidays": list(self.public_holidays), 
117:             "standard_daily_hours": self.standard_daily_hours, 
118:         } 
119:     @classmethod 
120:     def from_dict(cls, data): 
121:         cfg = cls(data["year"], data["month"]) 
122:         # open_hours 
123:         cfg.open_hours = { 
124:             int(k): tuple(v) 
125:             for k, v in data.get("open_hours", {}).items() 
126:         } 
127:         # niedziele handlowe 
128:         cfg.trade_sundays = set(data.get("trade_sundays", [])) 
129:         #święta ustawowo wolne 
130:         cfg.public_holidays = set(data.get("public_holidays", [])) 
131:         # override dni 
132:         cfg.day_overrides = { 
133:             int(day): tuple(hours) 
134:             for day, hours in data.get("day_overrides", {}).items() 
135:         } 
136:         # constraints 
137:         saved_constraints = data.get("constraints", {}) 
138:         cfg.constraints.update(saved_constraints) 
139:         # UI 
140:         cfg.cell_display_mode = data.get("cell_display_mode", "compact") 
141:         cfg.standard_daily_hours = data.get("standard_daily_hours", 8.0) 
142:         return cfg 
143:     def get_full_time_nominal_hours(self) -> int: 
144:         """ 
145:         Zwraca nominalny wymiar czasu pracy (pełny etat) 
146:         dla danego miesiąca zgodnie z kodeksem pracy. 
147:         """ 
148:         import calendar 
149:         from datetime import date 
150:         workdays = 0 
151:         days_in_month = calendar.monthrange(self.year, self.month)[1] 
152:         for d in range(1, days_in_month + 1): 
153:             wd = calendar.weekday(self.year, self.month, d) 
154:             # pon–pt 
155:             if wd < 5: 
156:                 # jeśli to święto ustawowe → nie liczymy 
157:                 if d in self.public_holidays: 
158:                     continue 
159:                 workdays += 1 
160:         return workdays * 8

6:         "schedule": schedule.to_dict(), 
7:         "shop_config": shop_config.to_dict() 
8:     }

10:         json.dump(data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) 
11: def load_project(path): 
12:     with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f: 
13:         data = json.load(f) 
14:     schedule = MonthSchedule.from_dict(data["schedule"]) 
15:     shop_config = ShopConfig.from_dict(data["shop_config"]) 
16:     return schedule, shop_config

1: import calendar 
2: import random 
3: import unittest 
4: try: 
5:     from ortools.sat.python import cp_model 
6:     from logic.auto_generator import AutoScheduleGenerator 
7:     from model.constraint_policy import ConstraintPolicy 
8:     from model.employee import Employee
