11:     HAS_ORTOOLS = True 
12: except ModuleNotFoundError: 
13:     HAS_ORTOOLS = False 
14: @unittest.skipUnless(HAS_ORTOOLS, "ortools is required for solver integration tests") 
15: class TestAutoScheduleGeneratorSolverEdgeCases(unittest.TestCase): 
16:     ACTIVE_DAYS = [3, 4, 5, 6, 7]  # celowo krótki horyzont dla szybszych testów 
17:     def _make_shop(self, year, month, rng): 
18:         shop = ShopConfig(year, month) 
19:         # Zostawiamy tylko kilka dni handlowych, resztę oznaczamy jako święta. 
20:         days_in_month = calendar.monthrange(year, month)[1] 
21:         shop.public_holidays = set(range(1, days_in_month + 1)) - set(self.ACTIVE_DAYS) 
22:         # Losowe godziny otwarcia (różne przypadki sklepów) 
23:         start = rng.choice(["05:30", "06:00", "06:30"]) 
24:         end = rng.choice(["20:00", "21:00", "22:00", "22:45"]) 
25:         for wd in range(7): 
26:             shop.open_hours[wd] = (start, end) 
27:         # Upraszczamy pozostałe constrainty, żeby testować głównie obsadę i role. 
28:         for key in ["rest_11h", "balance", "max_consecutive", "monthly_hours", "meat_coverage"]: 
29:             shop.constraint_policies[key] = ConstraintPolicy.DISABLED 
30:         shop.constraint_policies["open"] = ConstraintPolicy.MANDATORY 
31:         shop.constraint_policies["close"] = ConstraintPolicy.MANDATORY 
32:         shop.constraint_policies["meat"] = ConstraintPolicy.MANDATORY 
33:         return shop 
34:     def _build_case(self, rng, force_infeasible=False): 
35:         year, month = 2025, 2 
36:         schedule = MonthSchedule(year, month) 
37:         shop = self._make_shop(year, month, rng) 
38:         num_employees = rng.randint(5, 8) 
39:         if force_infeasible: 
40:             # Edge-case: za mało openerów i/lub mięsa + za wysoka wymagana obsada 
41:             opener_count = rng.randint(0, 1) 
42:             meat_count = rng.randint(0, 1) 
43:             min_open = rng.randint(3, 5) 
44:             min_close = rng.randint(3, 5) 
45:         else: 
46:             # Feasible: minimum 2 openerów i 2 mięsa (open + close każdego dnia) 
47:             opener_count = rng.randint(2, min(4, num_employees)) 
48:             meat_count = rng.randint(2, min(4, num_employees)) 
49:             min_open = rng.randint(2, 3) 
50:             min_close = rng.randint(2, 3) 
51:         opener_indices = set(rng.sample(range(num_employees), k=opener_count)) 
52:         meat_indices = set(rng.sample(range(num_employees), k=meat_count)) 
53:         for i in range(num_employees): 
54:             emp = Employee( 
55:                 last_name=f"Test{i}", 
56:                 first_name=f"Emp{i}", 
57:                 is_opener=i in opener_indices, 
58:                 is_meat=i in meat_indices, 
59:                 daily_hours=rng.randint(6, 8), 
60:             ) 
61:             schedule.add_employee(emp) 
62:         shop.constraints["min_open_staff"] = min_open 
63:         shop.constraints["min_close_staff"] = min_close 
64:         shop.constraints["max_consecutive_days"] = 10 
65:         case = { 
66:             "num_employees": num_employees, 
67:             "openers": opener_count, 
68:             "meat": meat_count, 
69:             "min_open": min_open, 
70:             "min_close": min_close, 
71:             "open_hours": shop.open_hours[0], 
72:             "active_days": list(self.ACTIVE_DAYS), 
73:             "force_infeasible": force_infeasible, 
74:         } 
75:         return schedule, shop, case 
76:     def test_solver_random_small_store_feasible_cases(self): 
77:         rng = random.Random(20250219) 
78:         iterations = 40 
79:         for idx in range(iterations): 
80:             schedule, shop, case = self._build_case(rng, force_infeasible=False) 
81:             gen = AutoScheduleGenerator(schedule, shop) 
82:             result = gen.generate() 
83:             self.assertTrue( 
84:                 result["success"], 
85:                 msg=f"Expected feasible but got infeasible at iter={idx}, case={case}, result={result}", 
86:             ) 
87:             self.assertIn(result["status"], (cp_model.OPTIMAL, cp_model.FEASIBLE)) 
88:     def test_solver_random_small_store_infeasible_cases_print_config(self): 
89:         rng = random.Random(20250220) 
90:         iterations = 60 
91:         infeasible_seen = 0 
92:         for idx in range(iterations): 
93:             schedule, shop, case = self._build_case(rng, force_infeasible=True) 
94:             gen = AutoScheduleGenerator(schedule, shop) 
95:             result = gen.generate() 
96:             if not result["success"]: 
97:                 infeasible_seen += 1 
98:                 print(f"[INFEASIBLE CASE {idx}] {case}") 
99:             self.assertFalse( 
100:                 result["success"], 
101:                 msg=f"Expected infeasible but solver found solution at iter={idx}, case={case}, result={result}", 
102:             ) 
103:         self.assertEqual( 
104:             infeasible_seen, 
105:             iterations, 
106:             msg="Każdy case w tym teście powinien być INFEASIBLE.", 
107:         ) 
108: if __name__ == "__main__": 
109:     unittest.main()

189:         layout.addLayout(form_staff)

191:         return page 
192:     def _save(self): 
193:         try: 
194:             for wd, (start_input, end_input) in self.open_edits.items(): 
195:                 start_str = start_input.get_time_str() 
196:                 end_str = end_input.get_time_str() 
197:

199:                 end_qt = _parse_time(end_str) 
200:                 if end_qt <= start_qt: 
201:                     day_names = ["Poniedziałek", "Wtorek", "Środa", "Czwartek", "Piątek", "Sobota", "Niedziela"] 
202:                     raise ValueError(f"Zamknięcie musi być później niż otwarcie w dniu: {day_names[wd]}.") 
203:                  
204:                 self.shop_config.open_hours[wd] = (start_str, end_str) 
205:             self.shop_config.trade_sundays = { 
206:                 day for day, box in self.sunday_checks.items() if box.isChecked() 
207:             } 
208:             self.shop_config.constraints["max_consecutive_days"] = self.max_consecutive.value() 
209:             self.shop_config.constraints["min_open_staff"] = self.min_open.value() 
210:             self.shop_config.constraints["min_close_staff"] = self.min_close.value() 
211:             self.shop_config.constraints["enforce_11h_rest"] = True 
212:             self.shop_config.constraints["enforce_meat_coverage"] = True 
213:             self.shop_config.constraints["force_fulltime_845"] = self.force_fulltime_845.isChecked() 
214:         except Exception as exc:

72:         buttons.rejected.connect(self.reject) 
73:         buttons.accepted.connect(self._save) 
74:         root.addWidget(buttons) 
75:     def _fill_values(self, start, end): 
76:         if start: 
77:             self.start_edit.set_time_str(start) 
78:         if end: 
79:             self._manual_end = True 
80:             self.end_edit.set_time_str(end) 
81:     def _suggest_end(self): 
82:         if self._manual_end: 
83:             self._update_duration() 
84:             return 
85:         start_qt = _parse_time(self.start_edit.get_time_str()) 
86:         suggested = start_qt.addSecs(self.daily_hours * 3600) 
87:          
88:         if suggested > self._open_end_qt: 
89:             suggested = self._open_end_qt 
90:         self._updating = True 
91:         self.end_edit.set_time_str(suggested.toString("HH:mm")) 
92:         self._updating = False 
93:         self._update_duration() 
94:     def _on_start_changed(self, _): 
95:         if self._updating: 
96:             return 
97:         if not self._manual_end: 
98:             self._suggest_end() 
99:         else: 
100:             self._update_duration() 
101:     def _on_end_changed(self, _): 
102:         if self._updating: 
103:             return 
104:         self._manual_end = True 
105:         self._update_duration() 
106:     def _update_duration(self): 
107:         start_qt = _parse_time(self.start_edit.get_time_str()) 
108:         end_qt = _parse_time(self.end_edit.get_time_str()) 
109:          
110:         minutes = start_qt.secsTo(end_qt) // 60 
111:         if minutes < 0: 
112:             minutes = 0 
113:         hours = minutes // 60 
114:         mins = minutes % 60 
115:         self.duration_label.setText(f"Czas pracy: {hours}:{mins:02d}") 
116:     def _set_free(self): 
117:         self.result_mode = "free" 
118:         self.accept() 
119:     def _set_leave(self): 
120:         self.result_mode = "leave" 
121:         self.accept() 
122:     def _set_sick(self): 
123:         self.result_mode = "sick" 
124:         self.accept() 
125:     def _save(self): 
126:         start_str = self.start_edit.get_time_str() 
127:         end_str = self.end_edit.get_time_str() 
128:          
129:         start_qt = _parse_time(start_str) 
130:         end_qt = _parse_time(end_str) 
131:         if end_qt <= start_qt: 
132:             QMessageBox.critical(self, "Błąd", "Koniec musi być później niż start.") 
133:             return 
134:         if start_qt < self._open_start_qt or end_qt > self._open_end_qt: 
135:             QMessageBox.critical(self, "Błąd", "Godziny muszą mieścić się w czasie otwarcia sklepu.") 
136:             return 
137:         self.result_mode = "hours" 
138:         self.result_start = start_str 
139:         self.result_end = end_str 
140:         self.accept()

83:         headers.extend(["Praca\n(h)", "Urlop\n(h)", "L4\n(h)", "Razem\n(h)"]) 
84:         self.setColumnCount(len(headers)) 
85:         self.setHorizontalHeaderLabels(headers) 
86:         self.setRowCount(len(self.schedule.employees) + 4) 
87:         self.setColumnWidth(0, 180) 
88:         for col in range(1, days + 1): 
89:             if self.compact_mode: 
90:                 self.setColumnWidth(col, 30) 
91:             else: 
92:                 self.setColumnWidth(col, 60) 
93:         for col in range(days + 1, days + 5): 
94:             self.setColumnWidth(col, 60) 
95:         self.verticalHeader().setVisible(False) 
96:         self.horizontalHeader().setDefaultAlignment(Qt.AlignCenter) 
97:         self.horizontalHeader().setStretchLastSection(False) 
98:         for row in range(self.rowCount()): 
99:             self.setRowHeight(row, 42) 
100:     def refresh(self): 
101:         if not self.schedule or not self.shop_config: 
102:             return 
103:         self.build() 
104:         presenter = SchedulePresenter(self.schedule, self.shop_config) 
105:         constraint_presenter = ConstraintPresenter(self.schedule, self.shop_config) 
106:         # 3. Flaga sprawdzania limitu dni pod rząd z konfiguracji (domyślnie False) 
107:         hl_consecutive = self.shop_config.constraints.get("highlight_max_consecutive", False) 
108:         days = self.schedule.days_in_month 
109:         emp_count = len(self.schedule.employees) 
110:         for row, emp in enumerate(self.schedule.employees): 
111:             self._fill_employee_name(row, emp) 
112:             self._fill_day_cells(row, emp, days, presenter, constraint_presenter, hl_consecutive) 
113:             self._fill_summary_cells(row, emp, days) 
114:         self._fill_validation_rows(emp_count, days, constraint_presenter) 
115:         self.viewport().update() 
116:     def _fill_employee_name(self, row, emp): 
117:         item = QTableWidgetItem(emp.display_name()) 
118:         item.setData(Qt.UserRole, emp) 
119:         item.setTextAlignment(Qt.AlignVCenter | Qt.AlignLeft) 
120:         if emp.is_opener and emp.is_meat: 
121:             size = 32 
122:             pixmap = QPixmap(size * 2, size) 
123:             pixmap.fill(Qt.transparent) 
124:             painter = QPainter(pixmap) 
125:             painter.drawPixmap(0, 0, self.icon_open.pixmap(size, size)) 
126:             painter.drawPixmap(size, 0, self.icon_meat.pixmap(size, size)) 
127:             painter.end() 
128:             item.setIcon(QIcon(pixmap)) 
129:             item.setIcon(self.icon_open_meat) 
130:         elif emp.is_opener: 
131:             item.setIcon(self.icon_open) 
132:         elif emp.is_meat: 
133:             item.setIcon(self.icon_meat) 
134:         font = QFont() 
135:         font.setBold(True) 
136:         item.setFont(font) 
137:         item.setBackground(QBrush(QColor(theme.BG_PANEL))) 
138:         self.setItem(row, 0, item) 
139:     def _fill_day_cells(self, row, emp, days, presenter, constraint_presenter, hl_consecutive): 
140:         for day in range(1, days + 1): 
141:             ds = self.schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
142:             item = QTableWidgetItem() 
143:             item.setTextAlignment(Qt.AlignHCenter | Qt.AlignVCenter) 
144:             item.setData(Qt.UserRole, (emp, day)) 
145:             if getattr(ds, "is_locked", False) and not ds.start and not ds.end and not ds.is_leave and not getattr(ds, "is_sick", False): 
146:                 item.setText("")  # Czyścimy tekst, żeby nie śmiecił 
147:                  
148:                 # Tworzymy profesjonalne szrafowanie (ukośne linie) 
149:                 brush = QBrush(QColor(205, 205, 205)) # Bardzo jasny szary 
150:                 brush.setStyle(Qt.BDiagPattern)       # Wzór: ukośne linie (Back Diagonal) 
151:                  
152:                 item.setBackground(brush) 
153:                 item.setToolTip("Dzień wolny (Zablokowany: Generator nie zmieni tego ustawienia)") 
154:                 self.setItem(row, day, item) 
155:                 continue 
156:             if hasattr(ds, "is_sick") and ds.is_sick: 
157:                 item.setText("🤒") 
158:                 item.setBackground(QBrush(QColor("#FFA07A"))) 
159:                 item.setToolTip("Chorobowe") 
160:                 self.setItem(row, day, item) 
161:                 continue 
162:             if ds.is_leave: 
163:                 item.setText("🌴") 
164:                 item.setBackground(QBrush(QColor(theme.OK_GREEN))) 
165:                 item.setToolTip("Urlop") 
166:                 self.setItem(row, day, item) 
167:                 continue 
168:             if not self.shop_config.is_trade_day(day): 
169:                 item.setBackground(QBrush(QColor(theme.BG_DISABLED))) 
170:                 self.setItem(row, day, item) 
171:                 continue 
172:             cell_view = presenter.get_cell_view(emp, day) 
173:             if self.compact_mode: 
174:                 text = "" 
175:                 hours = self.shop_config.get_open_hours_for_day(day) 
176:                 if hours and ds.start: 
177:                     open_start, open_end = hours 
178:                     from datetime import datetime 
179:                     fmt = "%H:%M" 
180:                     start = datetime.strptime(ds.start, fmt) 
181:                     shop_start = datetime.strptime(open_start, fmt) 
182:                     diff = (start - shop_start).total_seconds() / 60 
183:                     text = "2" if diff >= 120 else "1" 
184:                 item.setText(text) 
185:             else: 
186:                 lines = [line for line in [cell_view.text_start, cell_view.text_end, cell_view.text_total] if line] 
187:                 item.setText("\n".join(lines)) 
188:             item.setBackground(QBrush(QColor(cell_view.bg))) 
189:             if cell_view.tooltip: 
190:                 item.setToolTip(cell_view.tooltip) 
191:             # 3. Sprawdzanie błędów z flagą highlight_max_consecutive oraz zabezpieczenie przed błędem typu 
192:             error = constraint_presenter.get_cell_error(emp, day) 
193:             if error: 
194:                 is_cons_err = False 
195:                 if isinstance(error, str): 
196:                     is_cons_err = "dni pod rząd" in error.lower() 
197:                  
198:                 if not is_cons_err or hl_consecutive: 
199:                     item.setBackground(QBrush(QColor(theme.ERR_RED))) 
200:                     if isinstance(error, str): 
201:                         item.setToolTip(error) 
202:             self.setItem(row, day, item) 
203:     def _fill_summary_cells(self, row, emp, days): 
204:         items = [ 
205:             QTableWidgetItem(self.schedule.total_hours_for_employee(emp)), 
206:             QTableWidgetItem(self.schedule.leave_hours_for_employee(emp)), 
207:             QTableWidgetItem(self.schedule.sick_hours_for_employee(emp)), 
208:             QTableWidgetItem(self.schedule.total_with_leave_and_sick_for_employee(emp)), 
209:         ] 
210:         for idx, item in enumerate(items, start=days + 1): 
211:             item.setTextAlignment(Qt.AlignCenter) 
212:             item.setBackground(QBrush(QColor(theme.BG_PANEL))) 
213:             self.setItem(row, idx, item) 
214:     def _fill_validation_rows(self, emp_count, days, constraint_presenter): 
215:         # Definiujemy wiersze podsumowania 
216:         rows = [ 
217:             ("Otwarcie", "open"),  
218:             ("Zamknięcie", "close"),  
219:             ("Rano/Popo", "morning_afternoon"),  
220:             ("Mięso", "meat") 
221:         ] 
222:         for offset, (label, key) in enumerate(rows): 
223:             row = emp_count + offset 
224:             # Etykieta wiersza (lewa kolumna) 
225:             name_item = QTableWidgetItem(label) 
226:             name_item.setBackground(QBrush(QColor(theme.BG_HEADER))) 
227:             name_item.setTextAlignment(Qt.AlignVCenter | Qt.AlignLeft) 
228:             self.setItem(row, 0, name_item) 
229:             for day in range(1, days + 1): 
230:                 # Liczniki dla danego dnia 
231:                 at_opening = 0 
232:                 at_closing = 0 
233:                 total_morning = 0 
234:                 total_afternoon = 0 
235:                 count_meat = 0 
236:                 # Pobieramy godziny pracy sklepu z konfiguracji 
237:                 hours = self.shop_config.get_open_hours_for_day(day) 
238:                 if not hours: 
239:                     continue 
240:                 shop_open_str, shop_close_str = hours 
241:                  
242:                 try: 
243:                     shop_open_h = int(shop_open_str.split(":")[0]) 
244:                     shop_close_h = int(shop_close_str.split(":")[0]) 
245:                 except: 
246:                     continue 
247:                 for emp in self.schedule.employees: 
248:                     ds = self.schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
249:                      
250:                     # Ignorujemy osoby, które nie pracują, są na urlopie lub L4 
251:                     if not ds.start or ds.is_leave or getattr(ds, "is_sick", False): 
252:                         continue 
253:                     try: 
254:                         emp_start_h = int(ds.start.split(":")[0]) 
255:                         emp_end_h = int(ds.end.split(":")[0]) 
256:                         # --- LOGIKA ZGODNA Z GENERATOREM --- 
257:                          
258:                         # 1. Dokładne Otwarcie/Zamknięcie (walidacja) 
259:                         if ds.start == shop_open_str: 
260:                             at_opening += 1 
261:                         if ds.end == shop_close_str: 
262:                             at_closing += 1 
263:                         # 2. Rano / Popołudnie (wszystkie zmiany rano i po południu) 
264:                         # Rano: Zaczyna tak jak sklep LUB przed 12:00 
265:                         if emp_start_h <= shop_open_h or emp_start_h < 12: 
266:                             total_morning += 1 
267:                          
268:                         # Popołudnie: Kończy tak jak sklep LUB zaczyna od 12:00 wzwyż 
269:                         if emp_end_h >= shop_close_h or emp_start_h >= 12: 
270:                             total_afternoon += 1 
271:                         # 3. Mięso 
272:                         if emp.is_meat: 
273:                             count_meat += 1 
274:                     except: 
275:                         continue 
276:                 # Budowanie tekstu do wyświetlenia 
277:                 if key == "open": 
278:                     display_text = str(at_opening) 
279:                 elif key == "close": 
280:                     display_text = str(at_closing) 
281:                 elif key == "morning_afternoon": 
282:                     # Wyświetlamy w formacie Rano / Popo 
283:                     display_text = f"{total_morning}  /  {total_afternoon}" 
284:                 elif key == "meat": 
285:                     display_text = "✅" if count_meat > 0 else "❌" 
286:                 item = QTableWidgetItem(display_text) 
287:                 item.setTextAlignment(Qt.AlignCenter) 
288:                 # Kolorowanie tła 
289:                 if key == "morning_afternoon": 
290:                     # Wiersz informacyjny ma stały kolor panelu (taki jak prawidłowe otw/zam) 
291:                     item.setBackground(QBrush(QColor(theme.BG_PANEL))) 
292:                 else: 
293:                     # Reszta wierszy używa walidatora błędów 
294:                     view = constraint_presenter.get_validation_cell_view(key, day) 
295:                     item.setBackground(QBrush(QColor(view.bg))) 
296:                     if view.tooltip: 
297:                         item.setToolTip(view.tooltip) 
298:                 self.setItem(row, day, item) 
299:             # Wypełnienie komórek sumarycznych (ostatnie 4 kolumny) szarym kolorem 
300:             for col in range(days + 1, days + 5): 
301:                 filler = QTableWidgetItem("") 
302:                 filler.setBackground(QBrush(QColor(theme.BG_PANEL))) 
303:                 self.setItem(row, col, filler) 
304:     def paintEvent(self, event): 
305:         super().paintEvent(event) 
306:         painter = QPainter(self.viewport()) 
307:         painter.setRenderHint(QPainter.Antialiasing) 
308:         # 1. Obramówka aktywnego wiersza (grubsza) 
309:         if self.active_row is not None: 
310:             pen = QPen(QColor(0, 120, 215), 2) 
311:             painter.setPen(pen) 
312:             rect = self._get_full_row_rect(self.active_row) 
313:             painter.drawRect(rect.adjusted(1, 1, -1, -1)) 
314:         # 1. Obramówka najechanego wiersza (cieńsza, subtelniejsza) 
315:         if self.hovered_row is not None and self.hovered_row  
316:             pen = QPen(QColor(0, 120, 215, 80), 1) 
317:             painter.setPen(pen) 
318:             rect = self._get_full_row_rect(self.hovered_row) 
319:             painter.drawRect(rect.adjusted(1, 1, -1, -1)) 
320:     def _get_full_row_rect(self, row): 
321:         rect = self.visualRect(self.model().index(row, 0)) 
322:         for col in range(1, self.columnCount()): 
323:             rect = rect.united(self.visualRect(self.model().index(row, col))) 
324:         return rect 
325:     def _handle_click(self, row, col): 
326:         self.active_row = row 
327:         self.viewport().update() 
328:         if not self.schedule or not self.main_window: 
329:             return 
330:         emp_count = len(self.schedule.employees) 
331:         days = self.schedule.days_in_month 
332:         if row < emp_count and 1 <= col <= days: 
333:             if ( 
334:                 self.main_window.quick_mode_enabled 
335:                 and self.main_window.quick_selected_shift 
336:             ): 
337:                 self._apply_quick_shift(row, col) 
338:     def _handle_double_click(self, row, col): 
339:         if not self.schedule or not self.main_window: 
340:             return 
341:         emp_count = len(self.schedule.employees) 
342:         days = self.schedule.days_in_month 
343:         if row < emp_count and col == 0 and self.on_edit_employee: 
344:             self.on_edit_employee(self.schedule.employees[row]) 
345:             return 
346:         if row < emp_count and 1 <= col <= days: 
347:             if ( 
348:                 self.main_window.quick_mode_enabled 
349:                 and self.main_window.quick_selected_shift 
350:             ): 
351:                 self._apply_quick_shift(row, col) 
352:             elif self.on_edit_day: 
353:                 self.on_edit_day(self.schedule.employees[row], col) 
354:     def _handle_header_double_click(self, col): 
355:         # 4. Dwuklik na nagłówku 
356:         if 1 <= col <= self.schedule.days_in_month: 
357:             if self.on_header_menu: 
358:                 self.on_header_menu(col, None) 
359:     def contextMenuEvent(self, event): 
360:         # 100% pewna metoda na wyłapanie prawego przycisku myszy w Qt 
361:         global_pos = event.globalPos() 
362:          
363:         # Mapujemy globalną pozycję myszy na obszar viewportu tabeli 
364:         vp_pos = self.viewport().mapFromGlobal(global_pos) 
365:         row = self.rowAt(vp_pos.y()) 
366:         col = self.columnAt(vp_pos.x()) 
367:          
368:         if row == -1 or col == -1: 
369:             return 
370:              
371:         emp_count = len(self.schedule.employees) 
372:         days = self.schedule.days_in_month 
373:         if row >= emp_count or not (1 <= col <= days): 
374:             return 
375:         emp = self.schedule.employees[row] 
376:         day = col 
377:         ds = self.schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
378:          
379:         menu = QMenu(self) 
380:          
381:         act_copy = menu.addAction("Kopiuj dzień") 
382:         act_paste = menu.addAction("Wklej dzień") 
383:         act_paste.setEnabled(self._clipboard_day is not None) 
384:          
385:         menu.addSeparator() 
386:          
387:         act_unlock = menu.addAction("Odblokuj") 
388:         act_unlock.setEnabled(getattr(ds, "is_locked", False)) 
389:         action = menu.exec(global_pos) 
390:          
391:         if action == act_copy: 
392:             self._clipboard_day = { 
393:                 "start": ds.start, "end": ds.end,  
394:                 "is_leave": ds.is_leave, "is_sick": getattr(ds, "is_sick", False) 
395:             } 
396:             if self.main_window: 
397:                 self.main_window.statusBar().showMessage("Skopiowano dzień.", 2000) 
398:         elif action == act_paste: 
399:             self.controller.set_day_hours(emp, day, self._clipboard_day["start"], self._clipboard_day["end"]) 
400:             self.refresh() 
401:         elif action == act_unlock: 
402:             self.controller.snapshot() # Ręczny zapis przed manipulacją obiektem 
403:             ds.is_locked = False 
404:             self.refresh() 
405:     def _open_header_context_menu(self, pos): 
406:         # Zachowuję sygnaturę z Twojego oryginalnego kodu (teraz zastąpione przez double_click) 
407:         pass 
408:     def _apply_quick_shift(self, row, col): 
409:         if not self.main_window: 
410:             return 
411:         emp = self.schedule.employees[row] 
412:         day = col 
413:         shift = self.main_window.quick_selected_shift 
414:         start = None 
415:         end = None 
416:         if shift == "WORK": 
417:             # 🔥 Poprawione odwołanie do nowej metody w TimeInputWidget 
418:             start = self.main_window.start_input.get_time_str() 
419:             end = self.main_window.end_input.get_time_str() 
420:         elif shift == "SICK": 
421:             self.controller.snapshot() # Zabezpieczenie undo 
422:             ds = self.schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
423:             ds.is_locked = False 
424:             self.controller.set_day_sick(emp, day) 
425:             self.refresh() 
426:             return 
427:         elif shift == "OFF": 
428:             ds = self.schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
429:             # 🔥 jeśli już jest wolne → nic nie rób 
430:             if getattr(ds, "is_locked", False) and not ds.start and not ds.end and not ds.is_leave and not getattr(ds, "is_sick", False): 
431:                 return 
432:             self.controller.snapshot() # Zabezpieczenie undo 
433:             # 🔥 ustaw wolne ręczne 
434:             ds.start = None 
435:             ds.end = None 
436:             ds.is_leave = False 
437:             ds.is_sick = False 
438:             ds.is_locked = True 
439:             self.refresh() 
440:             return 
441:         ds = self.schedule.get_day(emp, day) 
442:         current = ( 
443:             ds.start, 
444:             ds.end, 
445:             ds.is_leave, 
446:             getattr(ds, "is_sick", False) 
447:         ) 
448:         new = (start, end, shift == "LEAVE", shift == "SICK") 
449:         if current == new: 
450:             return 
451:         self.controller.snapshot() # Zabezpieczenie undo 
452:         ds.is_locked = False 
453:         self.controller.set_shift(emp, day, shift, start, end) 
454:         self.refresh() 
455:     def set_clipboard(self, value): 
456:         self._clipboard_day = value 
457:     def clipboard(self): 
458:         return self._clipboard_day 
459:     def set_compact_mode(self, enabled: bool): 
460:         self.compact_mode = enabled 
461:         self.refresh()

284:         act_undo.triggered.connect(self._undo)

286:     def _init_state(self): 
287:         old_employees = [] 
288:         if self.schedule: 
289:             old_employees = self.schedule.employees 
290:         self.schedule = MonthSchedule(self.year, self.month, employees=old_employees) 
291:         self.shop_config = ShopConfig(self.year, self.month) 
292:         self.controller = ScheduleController(self.schedule, self.shop_config) 
293:     def _sync_everything(self): 
294:         self._sync_grid() 
295:         self._update_window_title() 
296:         self._update_state_label() 
297:     def _sync_grid(self): 
298:         self.grid.set_data( 
299:             self.schedule, 
300:             self.shop_config, 
301:             self.controller, 
302:             main_window=self, 
303:             on_edit_day=self._edit_day, 
304:             on_edit_employee=self._edit_employee, 
305:             on_context_menu=self._open_day_context_menu, 
306:             on_header_menu=self._open_header_menu, 
307:         ) 
308:         self.grid.build() 
309:         self.grid.refresh() 
310:     def _update_window_title(self): 
311:         self.setWindowTitle(f"Grafik Dino v2 — {self.month:02d}.{self.year}") 
312:     def _update_nominal_hours_label(self): 
313:         if not self.shop_config: 
314:             self.nominal_hours_label.setText("-") 
315:             return 
316:         hours = self.shop_config.get_full_time_nominal_hours() 
317:         self.nominal_hours_label.setText(f"{hours} h") 
318:     def _update_state_label(self): 
319:         if not self.schedule: 
320:             self.state_label.setText("") 
321:             return 
322:         self.state_label.setText(f"{self.month:02d}.{self.year}") 
323:     def _set_date_controls(self, year, month): 
324:         self._loading = True 
325:         self.year_spin.blockSignals(True) 
326:         self.month_spin.blockSignals(True) 
327:         self.year_spin.setValue(year) 
328:         self.month_spin.setValue(month) 
329:         self.year_spin.blockSignals(False) 
330:         self.month_spin.blockSignals(False) 
331:         self._loading = False 
332:     def _on_date_change(self): 
333:         if self._loading: 
334:             return 
335:         self.year = self.year_spin.value() 
336:         self.month = self.month_spin.value() 
337:         self._init_state() 
338:         self._update_nominal_hours_label() 
339:         self._sync_everything() 
340:         self.statusBar().showMessage("Utworzono nowy grafik dla wybranego miesiąca.", 2500) 
341:     def _generate_schedule(self): 
342:         if not self.schedule.employees: 
343:             QMessageBox.information(self, "Generowanie", "Dodaj pracowników przed generowaniem grafiku.") 
344:             return 
345:         self._show_loading() 
346:         self.thread = QThread() 
347:         self.worker = GeneratorWorker(self.controller) 
348:         self.worker.moveToThread(self.thread) 
349:         self.thread.started.connect(self.worker.run) 
350:         self.worker.finished.connect(self._on_generation_finished) 
351:         self.worker.finished.connect(self.thread.quit) 
352:         self.worker.finished.connect(self.worker.deleteLater) 
353:         self.thread.finished.connect(self.thread.deleteLater) 
354:         self.thread.start() 
355:     def _on_generation_finished(self, result): 
356:         self._hide_loading() 
357:         self.schedule = self.controller.schedule 
358:         self._sync_everything() 
359:         if result and result.get("success"): 
360:             self.statusBar().showMessage("Grafik wygenerowany.", 3000) 
361:             QMessageBox.information(self, "Sukces", "Grafik został wygenerowany.") 
362:         else: 
363:             QMessageBox.warning(self, "Brak rozwiązania", "Nie udało się znaleźć poprawnego grafiku.") 
364:     def _open_add_employee(self): 
365:         dialog = EmployeeDialog(self) 
366:         if dialog.exec()  
367:             return 
368:         self.controller.add_employee(dialog.employee_result) 
369:         self.schedule = self.controller.schedule 
370:         self._sync_everything() 
371:         self.statusBar().showMessage("Dodano pracownika.", 2500) 
372:     def _edit_employee(self, emp): 
373:         dialog = EmployeeDialog(self, employee=emp) 
374:         if dialog.exec()  
375:             return 
376:         if dialog.employee_result is None: 
377:             self.controller.remove_employee(emp) 
378:             self.schedule = self.controller.schedule 
379:             self._sync_everything() 
380:             self.statusBar().showMessage("Usunięto pracownika.", 2500) 
381:             return 
382:         self.controller.replace_employee(emp, dialog.employee_result) 
383:         self.schedule = self.controller.schedule 
384:         self._sync_everything() 
385:         self.statusBar().showMessage("Zapisano pracownika.", 2500) 
386:     def _edit_day(self, emp, day): 
387:         hours = self.shop_config.get_open_hours_for_day(day) 
388:         if not hours: 
389:             return 
390:         ds = self.controller.get_day(emp, day) 
391:         dialog = DayEditDialog( 
392:             self, 
393:             start=None if ds.is_leave else ds.start, 
394:             end=None if ds.is_leave else ds.end, 
395:             open_start=hours[0], 
396:             open_end=hours[1], 
397:             daily_hours=emp.daily_hours, 
398:         ) 
399:         if dialog.exec()  
400:             return 
401:         if dialog.result_mode == "free": 
402:             self.controller.set_day_free(emp, day) 
403:         elif dialog.result_mode == "leave": 
404:             self.controller.set_day_leave(emp, day) 
405:         elif dialog.result_mode == "sick": 
406:             self.controller.set_day_sick(emp, day) 
407:         elif dialog.result_mode == "hours": 
408:             self.controller.set_day_hours(emp, day, dialog.result_start, dialog.result_end) 
409:         self.schedule = self.controller.schedule 
410:         self._sync_everything() 
411:         self.statusBar().showMessage("Zmieniono dzień.", 2500) 
412:     def _open_day_context_menu(self, emp, day, global_pos): 
413:         if not self.shop_config.is_trade_day(day): 
414:             return 
415:         menu = QMenu(self) 
416:         menu.addAction("Rano", lambda: self._ctx_morning(emp, day)) 
417:         menu.addAction("Zamknięcie", lambda: self._ctx_close(emp, day)) 
418:         menu.addSeparator() 
419:         menu.addAction("Kopiuj dzień", lambda: self._ctx_copy(emp, day)) 
420:         menu.addAction("Wklej dzień", lambda: self._ctx_paste(emp, day)) 
421:         menu.addSeparator() 
422:         menu.addAction("Ustaw wolne", lambda: self._ctx_free(emp, day)) 
423:         menu.addAction("Ustaw urlop", lambda: self._ctx_leave(emp, day)) 
424:         menu.exec(global_pos) 
425:     def _ctx_copy(self, emp, day): 
426:         ds = self.controller.get_day(emp, day) 
427:         if ds.is_empty(): 
428:             self._clipboard_day = None 
429:             self.grid.set_clipboard(None) 
430:             return 
431:         self._clipboard_day = { 
432:             "start": ds.start, 
433:             "end": ds.end, 
434:             "is_leave": ds.is_leave, 
435:         } 
436:         self.grid.set_clipboard(self._clipboard_day) 
437:         self.statusBar().showMessage("Skopiowano dzień.", 1800) 
438:     def _ctx_paste(self, emp, day): 
439:         clip = self.grid.clipboard() or self._clipboard_day 
440:         if not clip: 
441:             return 
442:         if clip.get("is_leave"): 
443:             self.controller.set_day_leave(emp, day) 
444:         else: 
445:             self.controller.set_day_hours(emp, day, clip["start"], clip["end"]) 
446:         self.schedule = self.controller.schedule 
447:         self._sync_everything() 
448:     def _ctx_free(self, emp, day): 
449:         self.controller.set_day_free(emp, day) 
450:         self.schedule = self.controller.schedule 
451:         self._sync_everything() 
452:     def _ctx_leave(self, emp, day): 
453:         self.controller.set_day_leave(emp, day) 
454:         self.schedule = self.controller.schedule 
455:         self._sync_everything() 
456:     def _ctx_sick(self, emp, day): 
457:         self.controller.set_day_sick(emp, day) 
458:         self.schedule = self.controller.schedule 
459:         self._sync_everything() 
460:     def _ctx_morning(self, emp, day): 
461:         hours = self.shop_config.get_open_hours_for_day(day) 
462:         if not hours: 
463:             return 
464:         start = hours[0] 
465:         end = self._calc_end_from_daily(start, emp.daily_hours) 
466:         self.controller.set_day_hours(emp, day, start, end) 
467:         self.schedule = self.controller.schedule 
468:         self._sync_everything() 
469:     def _ctx_close(self, emp, day): 
470:         hours = self.shop_config.get_open_hours_for_day(day) 
471:         if not hours: 
472:             return 
473:         end = hours[1] 
474:         start = self._calc_start_from_daily(end, emp.daily_hours) 
475:         self.controller.set_day_hours(emp, day, start, end) 
476:         self.schedule = self.controller.schedule 
477:         self._sync_everything() 
478:     def _open_header_menu(self, day, global_pos): 
479:         hours = self.shop_config.get_open_hours_for_day(day) 
480:         if not hours: 
481:             weekday = self.shop_config.weekday(day) 
482:             hours = self.shop_config.get_open_hours_for_weekday(weekday) 
483:         dialog = DayOverrideDialog(self, day, hours, self.shop_config) 
484:         result = dialog.exec() 
485:         if result  
486:             return 
487:         if dialog.result_mode == "reset": 
488:             self.shop_config.day_overrides.pop(day, None) 
489:             self.shop_config.public_holidays.discard(day) 
490:         elif dialog.result_mode == "save": 
491:             self.shop_config.day_overrides[day] = (dialog.result_start, dialog.result_end) 
492:             if dialog.result_holiday: 
493:                 self.shop_config.public_holidays.add(day) 
494:             else: 
495:                 self.shop_config.public_holidays.discard(day) 
496:         self._update_nominal_hours_label() 
497:         self._sync_grid() 
498:         self.statusBar().showMessage("Zaktualizowano godziny dnia.", 2500) 
499:     def _open_config(self): 
500:         dialog = ConfigDialog(self, self.shop_config) 
501:         if dialog.exec()  
502:             return 
503:         self._update_nominal_hours_label() 
504:         self._sync_grid() 
505:         self.statusBar().showMessage("Zapisano konfigurację.", 2500) 
506:     def _save_project(self): 
507:         path, _ = QFileDialog.getSaveFileName(self, "Zapisz projekt", "", "Projekt grafiku (*.json)") 
508:         if not path: 
509:             return 
510:         save_project(path, self.schedule, self.shop_config) 
511:         save_project("last_project.json", self.schedule, self.shop_config) 
512:         self.statusBar().showMessage("Zapisano projekt.", 2500) 
513:     def _load_project(self): 
514:         path, _ = QFileDialog.getOpenFileName(self, "Wczytaj projekt", "", "Projekt grafiku (*.json)") 
515:         if not path: 
516:             return 
517:         self.schedule, self.shop_config = load_project(path) 
518:         self.controller = ScheduleController(self.schedule, self.shop_config) 
519:         self.year = self.schedule.year 
520:         self.month = self.schedule.month 
521:         self._set_date_controls(self.year, self.month) 
522:         self._update_nominal_hours_label() 
523:         self._sync_everything() 
524:         self.statusBar().showMessage("Wczytano projekt.", 2500) 
525:     def _export_excel(self): 
526:         path, _ = QFileDialog.getSaveFileName(self, "Eksport Excel", "", "Excel (*.xlsx)") 
527:         if not path: 
528:             return 
529:         export_schedule_to_excel(self.schedule, self.year, self.month, path) 
530:         self.statusBar().showMessage("Wyeksportowano do Excela.", 2500) 
531:     def _export_image(self): 
532:         path, _ = QFileDialog.getSaveFileName(self, "Eksport JPG", "", "Obraz JPG (*.jpg)") 
533:         if not path: 
534:             return 
535:         if not path.lower().endswith(".jpg"): 
536:             path += ".jpg" 
537:         export_schedule_to_image(self.schedule, self.year, self.month, path) 
538:         self.statusBar().showMessage("Wyeksportowano do JPG.", 2500) 
539:     def _undo(self): 
540:         self.schedule = self.controller.undo() 
541:         self._sync_everything() 
542:         self.statusBar().showMessage("Cofnięto ostatnią zmianę.", 2500) 
543:     def _about(self): 
544:         QMessageBox.information(self, "O programie", "Grafik Dino v2\nNowe UI w PySide6.") 
545:     def _try_load_last_project(self): 
546:         if not os.path.exists("last_project.json"): 
547:             return 
548:         try: 
549:             self.schedule, self.shop_config = load_project("last_project.json") 
550:             self.controller = ScheduleController(self.schedule, self.shop_config) 
551:             self.year = self.schedule.year 
552:             self.month = self.schedule.month 
553:             self._set_date_controls(self.year, self.month) 
554:             self._update_nominal_hours_label() 
555:             self._sync_everything() 
556:         except Exception: 
557:             pass 
558:     def _toggle_compact_mode(self, checked): 
559:         self.grid.set_compact_mode(checked) 
560:         self.statusBar().showMessage( 
561:             "Tryb kompaktowy włączony." if checked else "Tryb kompaktowy wyłączony.", 
562:             2000 
563:         ) 
564:     def _toggle_quick_mode(self): 
565:         self.quick_mode_enabled = self.btn_quick_mode.isChecked() 
566:         self._update_quick_mode_ui() 
567:     def _update_quick_mode_ui(self): 
568:         if self.quick_mode_enabled: 
569:             self.quick_panel.show() 
570:         else: 
571:             self.quick_panel.hide() 
572:     def _set_quick_shift(self, shift_type): 
573:         self.quick_selected_shift = shift_type 
574:         # reset 
575:         self.btn_work.setChecked(False) 
576:         self.btn_off.setChecked(False) 
577:         self.btn_leave.setChecked(False) 
578:         self.btn_sick.setChecked(False) 
579:         # aktywny 
580:         if shift_type == "WORK": 
581:             self.btn_work.setChecked(True) 
582:             self.time_panel.show() 
583:         elif shift_type == "OFF": 
584:             self.btn_off.setChecked(True) 
585:             self.time_panel.hide() 
586:         elif shift_type == "LEAVE": 
587:             self.btn_leave.setChecked(True) 
588:             self.time_panel.hide() 
589:         elif shift_type == "SICK": 
590:             self.btn_sick.setChecked(True) 
591:             self.time_panel.hide() 
592:     def _calc_end_from_daily(self, start_str, hours): 
593:         from datetime import datetime, timedelta 
594:         fmt = "%H:%M" 
595:         start = datetime.strptime(start_str, fmt) 
596:         end = start + timedelta(hours=hours) 
597:         return end.strftime(fmt) 
598:     def _calc_start_from_daily(self, end_str, hours): 
599:         from datetime import datetime, timedelta 
600:         fmt = "%H:%M" 
601:         end = datetime.strptime(end_str, fmt) 
602:         start = end - timedelta(hours=hours) 
603:         return start.strftime(fmt) 
604:     def _open_tutorial(self): 
605:         from ui.tutorial_dialog import TutorialDialog 
606:         dialog = TutorialDialog(self) 
607:         dialog.exec() 
608:     def _build_loading_overlay(self): 
609:         self.loading_overlay = QWidget(self) 
610:         self.loading_overlay.setStyleSheet("background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 120);") 
611:         self.loading_overlay.hide() 
612:         layout = QVBoxLayout(self.loading_overlay) 
613:         layout.setAlignment(Qt.AlignCenter) 
614:         self.spinner = LoadingSpinner(self) 
615:         layout.addWidget(self.spinner, alignment=Qt.AlignCenter) 
616:         self.loading_label = QLabel("Generowanie grafiku...") 
617:         self.loading_label.setStyleSheet("color: white; font-size: 20px;") 
618:         self.loading_label.setAlignment(Qt.AlignCenter) 
619:         layout.addWidget(self.loading_label) 
620:     def _show_loading(self): 
621:         self.loading_overlay.setGeometry(self.rect()) 
622:         self.loading_overlay.show() 
623:         QApplication.processEvents() 
624:     def _hide_loading(self): 
625:         self.loading_overlay.hide() 
626:     def _ctx_sick(self, emp, day): 
627:         self.controller.set_day_sick(emp, day) 
628:         self.schedule = self.controller.schedule 
629:         self._sync_everything() 
630: from PySide6.QtCore import QTimer 
631: class LoadingSpinner(QWidget): 
632:     def __init__(self, parent=None): 
633:         super().__init__(parent) 
634:         self._angle = 0 
635:         self._timer = QTimer(self) 
636:         self._timer.timeout.connect(self._rotate) 
637:         self._timer.start(16)  # ~60 FPS 
638:         self.setFixedSize(80, 80) 
639:     def _rotate(self): 
640:         self._angle = (self._angle + 5) % 360 
641:         self.update() 
642:     def paintEvent(self, event): 
643:         painter = QPainter(self) 
644:         painter.setRenderHint(QPainter.Antialiasing) 
645:         rect = self.rect().adjusted(10, 10, -10, -10) 
646:         # tło (szare kółko) 
647:         painter.setPen(QColor(255, 255, 255, 40)) 
648:         painter.drawEllipse(rect) 
649:         # aktywny łuk 
650:         pen = painter.pen() 
651:         pen.setWidth(4) 
652:         pen.setColor(QColor(255, 255, 255)) 
653:         painter.setPen(pen) 
654:         painter.drawArc(rect, int(self._angle * 16), int(120 * 16))

1: from PySide6.QtWidgets import QWidget, QHBoxLayout, QSpinBox, QLabel 
2: from PySide6.QtCore import Qt 
3: class CleanSpinBox(QSpinBox): 
4:     def __init__(self, parent=None): 
5:         super().__init__(parent) 
6:         self.setButtonSymbols(QSpinBox.NoButtons) 
7:         self.setAlignment(Qt.AlignCenter) 
8:         self.setMinimumHeight(30) 
9:         self.setStyleSheet(""" 
10:             QSpinBox { 
11:                 border: 1px solid #ccc; 
12:                 border-radius: 4px; 
13:                 background: white; 
14:                 padding: 2px; 
15:                 font-size: 14px; 
16:                 selection-background-color: #0078d4;  
17:                 selection-color: white; 
18:             } 
19:             QSpinBox:focus { 
20:                 border: 2px solid #0078d4; 
21:                 background-color: #f0f7ff; 
22:             } 
23:         """) 
24:     def keyPressEvent(self, event): 
25:         if event.key() in (Qt.Key_Return, Qt.Key_Enter): 
26:             self.focusNextChild() 
27:         else: 
28:             super().keyPressEvent(event) 
29: class TimeInputWidget(QWidget): 
30:     def __init__(self, parent=None): 
31:         super().__init__(parent) 
32:         layout = QHBoxLayout(self) 
33:         layout.setContentsMargins(0, 0, 0, 0) 
34:         layout.setSpacing(4) 
35:         # Ustawienie wyrównania layoutu do środka, aby elementy nie "uciekały" od siebie 
36:         layout.setAlignment(Qt.AlignCenter) 
37:         self.hour_box = CleanSpinBox() 
38:         self.hour_box.setRange(0, 23) 
39:         self.hour_box.setFixedWidth(45) 
40:         self.hour_box.textFromValue = lambda v: f"{v:02d}" 
41:         self.minute_box = CleanSpinBox() 
42:         self.minute_box.setRange(0, 59) 
43:         self.minute_box.setSingleStep(5) 
44:         self.minute_box.setFixedWidth(45) 
45:         self.minute_box.textFromValue = lambda v: f"{v:02d}" 
46:         layout.addWidget(self.hour_box) 
47:          
48:         colon = QLabel(":") 
49:         colon.setStyleSheet("font-weight: bold; font-size: 14px;") 
50:         layout.addWidget(colon) 
51:          
52:         layout.addWidget(self.minute_box) 
53:     def get_time_str(self): 
54:         return f"{self.hour_box.value():02d}:{self.minute_box.value():02d}" 
55:     def set_time_str(self, time_str): 
56:         if not time_str: 
57:             return 
58:         try: 
59:             h, m = map(int, time_str.split(":")) 
60:             self.hour_box.setValue(h) 
61:             self.minute_box.setValue(m) 
62:         except ValueError: 
63:             pass

FILE: C:\Users\kewi1\Desktop\Grafik dino V2\ui\tooltip.py 
================================================== 
 
1: import tkinter as tk 
2: class Tooltip: 
3:     def __init__(self, widget, text: str): 
4:         self.widget = widget 
5:         self.text = text 
6:         self.tip = None 
7:         # zapamiętaj ID bindingów 
8:         self._enter_id = widget.bind("<Enter>", self.show) 
9:         self._leave_id = widget.bind("<Leave>", self.hide) 
10:     def show(self, _=None): 
11:         if self.tip or not self.text: 
12:             return 
13:         x = self.widget.winfo_rootx() + 15 
14:         y = self.widget.winfo_rooty() + 15 
15:         self.tip = tk.Toplevel(self.widget) 
16:         self.tip.wm_overrideredirect(True) 
17:         self.tip.wm_geometry(f"+{x}+{y}") 
18:         tk.Label( 
19:             self.tip, 
20:             text=self.text, 
21:             background="#ffffe0", 
22:             relief="solid", 
23:             borderwidth=1, 
24:             font=("Arial", 9) 
25:         ).pack() 
26:     def hide(self, _=None): 
27:         if self.tip: 
28:             self.tip.destroy() 
29:             self.tip = None 
30:     def destroy(self): 
31:         # usuń tooltip jeśli widoczny 
32:         self.hide() 
33:         # odłącz bindingi 
34:         if self._enter_id: 
35:             self.widget.unbind("<Enter>", self._enter_id) 
36:         if self._leave_id: 
37:             self.widget.unbind("<Leave>", self._leave_id)
